§ 1

p.1, l.1

  • (p.1, l.1)madhyāhnārkamarīcikāsv iva payaḥpūro yad ajñānataḥ,khaṃ vāyur jvalano jalaṃ kṣitir iti trailokyam unmīlati | yat tattvaṃ viduṣāṃ nimīlati punaḥ, sragbhogibhogopamaṃ,sāndrānandam upāsmahe tad amalaṃ svātmāvabodhaṃ mahaḥ ||
  • api ca —
  • antarnāḍīniyamitamarullaṅghitabrahmarandhraṃ,svānte śāntipraṇayini samunmīlad ānandasāndram,pratyagjyotir jayati yaminaḥ spaṣṭalālāṭanetravyājavyaktikṛtam iva jagad vyāpi candrārdhamauleḥ ||
madhyāhnārkamarīcikāsv iva payaḥpūro yad ajñānataḥ,khaṃ vāyur jvalano jalaṃ kṣitir iti trailokyam unmīlati | yat tattvaṃ viduṣāṃ nimīlati punaḥ, sragbhogibhogopamaṃ,sāndrānandam upāsmahe tad amalaṃ svātmāvabodhaṃ mahaḥ ||

api ca —

antarnāḍīniyamitamarullaṅghitabrahmarandhraṃ,svānte śāntipraṇayini samunmīlad ānandasāndram,pratyagjyotir jayati yaminaḥ spaṣṭalālāṭanetravyājavyaktikṛtam iva jagad vyāpi candrārdhamauleḥ ||

nāndyante tataḥ praviṣati sūtradhāraḥ |

((nāndyante tataḥ praviṣati sūtradhāraḥ |))

sūtradhāraḥ

alam ativistareṇa! ādiṣṭo 'smi — sakalasāmantacakracūḍāmaṇimarīcimañjarīnīrājitacaraṇakamalena; balavadarinivahavakṣaḥsthalakavāṭapāṭanaprakaṭitanṛsiṃharūpeṇa; prabalataranarapatikulapralayamahārṇavanimagnamedinīsamuddharaṇopanītamahāvaraharūpeṇa; sakaladigvilāsinīkarṇapūrīkṛtakīrtilatāpallavena; samastāśāstamberamakarṇatālāsphālanabahalapavanasampātapravardhitapratāpānalena — śrīmatā gopalena, yathā khalv — «asya sahajasuhṛdo rājñaḥ kīrtivarmadevasya digvijayavyāpārāntaritaparabrahmānandair asmābhiḥ samunmīlitavividhaviṣamaviṣayarasāsvādadūṣitā ivātivāhitā divasāḥ | idānīṃ tu kṛtakṛtyā vayam | yataḥ —

  • nītāḥ kṣayaṃ kṣitibhujo nṛpater vipakṣā;rakṣāvatī kṣitir abhūt prathitair amātyaiḥ | sāmrājyam asya vihitaṃ kṣitipālamaulimālārpitaṃ bhuvi payonidhimekhalāyām ||

    • tad vayaṃ śāntarasaprayogābhinayenātmānaṃ vinodayitum icchāmaḥ | tad yat pūrvam asmadgurubhis, tatrabhavadbhiḥ śrīkṛṣṇamiśraiḥ prabodhacandrodayaṃ nāma nāṭakaṃ nirmāya bhavataḥ samarpitam āsīt tad adya rājñaḥ śrīkīrtivarmaṇaḥ purastād abhinetavyaṃ bhavatā | asti cāsya bhūpateḥ sapariṣadas tadavalokane kutūhalam» iti | tad bhavatu | gṛhaṃ gatvā, gṛhiṇīm āhūya, saṅgītakam anutiṣṭhāmi | parikramya, nepathyābhimukham avalokya | ārye! itas tāvat! praviśya |

    sūtradhāraḥ — alam ativistareṇa! ādiṣṭo 'smi — sakalasāmantacakracūḍāmaṇimarīcimañjarīnīrājitacaraṇakamalena; balavadarinivahavakṣaḥsthalakavāṭapāṭanaprakaṭitanṛsiṃharūpeṇa; prabalataranarapatikulapralayamahārṇavanimagnamedinīsamuddharaṇopanītamahāvaraharūpeṇa; sakaladigvilāsinīkarṇapūrīkṛtakīrtilatāpallavena; samastāśāstamberamakarṇatālāsphālanabahalapavanasampātapravardhitapratāpānalena — śrīmatā gopalena, yathā khalv — «asya sahajasuhṛdo rājñaḥ kīrtivarmadevasya digvijayavyāpārāntaritaparabrahmānandair asmābhiḥ samunmīlitavividhaviṣamaviṣayarasāsvādadūṣitā ivātivāhitā divasāḥ | idānīṃ tu kṛtakṛtyā vayam | yataḥ —

    nītāḥ kṣayaṃ kṣitibhujo nṛpater vipakṣā;rakṣāvatī kṣitir abhūt prathitair amātyaiḥ | sāmrājyam asya vihitaṃ kṣitipālamaulimālārpitaṃ bhuvi payonidhimekhalāyām ||

    tad vayaṃ śāntarasaprayogābhinayenātmānaṃ vinodayitum icchāmaḥ | tad yat pūrvam asmadgurubhis, tatrabhavadbhiḥ śrīkṛṣṇamiśraiḥ prabodhacandrodayaṃ nāma nāṭakaṃ nirmāya bhavataḥ samarpitam āsīt tad adya rājñaḥ śrīkīrtivarmaṇaḥ purastād abhinetavyaṃ bhavatā | asti cāsya bhūpateḥ sapariṣadas tadavalokane kutūhalam» iti | tad bhavatu | gṛhaṃ gatvā, gṛhiṇīm āhūya, saṅgītakam anutiṣṭhāmi | ((parikramya, nepathyābhimukham avalokya |)) ārye! itas tāvat! ((praviśya |))

    naṭī

    esa mhi | āṇavedu, ayyaütto, ko ṇioo aṇuciṭṭhīyadu tti |eṣāsmi | ājñāpayatv āryaputraḥ ko niyogo 'nuṣṭhīyatām iti |

    naṭī — esa mhi | āṇavedu, ayyaütto, ko ṇioo aṇuciṭṭhīyadu tti | (eṣāsmi | ājñāpayatv āryaputraḥ ko niyogo 'nuṣṭhīyatām iti |)

    sūtradhāraḥ

    ārye viditam eva bhavatyā —

  • asti pratyarthipṛthvīpativipulabalāraṇyamūrcchatpratāpajyotirjvālāvalīḍhatribhuvanavivaro viśvaviśrāntakīrtiḥ | gopālo bhūmipālān prasabham asilatāmitramātreṇa jitvā;sāmrājye kīrtivarmā narapatitilako yena bhūyo 'bhyaṣeci ||
  • api ca —
  • adyāpy unmadayātudhānataruṇīcañcatkarāsphālanavyāvalgannṛkapālatālaraṇitair nṛtyatpiśācāṅganāḥ | udgāyanti yaśāṃsi yasya vitatair nādaiḥ pracaṇḍānilaprakṣubhyatkarikumbhakūṭakuharavyaktai raṇakṣoṇayaḥ ||

    • tena ca śāntapathaprasthitenātmano vinodārthaṃ prabodhacandrodayābhidhānaṃ nāṭakam abhinetum ādiṣṭo 'smi | tad ādiśyantāṃ bharatā varṇikāparigrahāya!

    sūtradhāraḥ — ārye viditam eva bhavatyā —

    asti pratyarthipṛthvīpativipulabalāraṇyamūrcchatpratāpajyotirjvālāvalīḍhatribhuvanavivaro viśvaviśrāntakīrtiḥ | gopālo bhūmipālān prasabham asilatāmitramātreṇa jitvā;sāmrājye kīrtivarmā narapatitilako yena bhūyo 'bhyaṣeci ||

    api ca —

    adyāpy unmadayātudhānataruṇīcañcatkarāsphālanavyāvalgannṛkapālatālaraṇitair nṛtyatpiśācāṅganāḥ | udgāyanti yaśāṃsi yasya vitatair nādaiḥ pracaṇḍānilaprakṣubhyatkarikumbhakūṭakuharavyaktai raṇakṣoṇayaḥ ||

    tena ca śāntapathaprasthitenātmano vinodārthaṃ prabodhacandrodayābhidhānaṃ nāṭakam abhinetum ādiṣṭo 'smi | tad ādiśyantāṃ bharatā varṇikāparigrahāya!

    naṭī

    savismayam accariaṃ accariaṃ | jeṇa taha ṇiabhuabalavikkam'ekkaṇibbhacchiasaalarāamaṇḍaleṇa ākaṇṇākiṭṭhakaṭhiṇakoaṇḍadaṇḍabahalaghaṇavarisantasantaasaradhārāṇiarajajjarijjantaturaṃataraṃamālaṃ, ṇirantaraṇivaḍantatikkhakhaggavikkhattasahatthasathapaliattotuṅgamaāṅgamahāmahīharasahassaṃ, bhamantabhuadaṇḍamandalāhihādaghuṇṇantasaalapattisalilasaṇghāaṃ, kaṇṇaseṇṇasāaraṃ ṇimmahia | mahumahaṇeṇavva khīrasamuddaṃ āsādiā; samaravijaalacchī | tassa saṃpadaṃ saalamuṇiaṇasalāṇijjo kahaṃ īriso uvasamo saṃvutto |āścaryam, āścaryam! yena tathā nijabhujabalavikram'aikanirbhartsitasakalarājamaṇḍalenākarṇākṛṣṭakaṭhinakodaṇḍadaṇḍabahalaghanavarṣatsantataśaradhārānikarajarjaratturaṅgataraṅgamālaṃ nirantaranipatattīkṣṇakhadgavikṣiptasvahastaśastraparyastottuṅgamātaṅgamahāmahīdharasahasram bhramadbhujadaṇḍamandarābhighātaghūrṇamānasakalapattisalilasaṃghātaṃ karṇasainyasāgaraṃ nirmathya madhumathaneneva kṣīrasamudram āsāditā samaravijayalakṣmīḥ | tasya sāmprataṃ sakalamunijanaślāghanīyaḥ katham īdṛśa upaśamaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ |

    naṭī — ((savismayam))accariaṃ accariaṃ | jeṇa taha ṇiabhuabalavikkam'ekkaṇibbhacchiasaalarāamaṇḍaleṇa ākaṇṇākiṭṭhakaṭhiṇakoaṇḍadaṇḍabahalaghaṇavarisantasantaasaradhārāṇiarajajjarijjantaturaṃataraṃamālaṃ, ṇirantaraṇivaḍantatikkhakhaggavikkhattasahatthasathapaliattotuṅgamaāṅgamahāmahīharasahassaṃ, bhamantabhuadaṇḍamandalāhihādaghuṇṇantasaalapattisalilasaṇghāaṃ, kaṇṇaseṇṇasāaraṃ ṇimmahia | mahumahaṇeṇavva khīrasamuddaṃ āsādiā; samaravijaalacchī | tassa saṃpadaṃ saalamuṇiaṇasalāṇijjo kahaṃ īriso uvasamo saṃvutto | (āścaryam, āścaryam! yena tathā nijabhujabalavikram'aikanirbhartsitasakalarājamaṇḍalenākarṇākṛṣṭakaṭhinakodaṇḍadaṇḍabahalaghanavarṣatsantataśaradhārānikarajarjaratturaṅgataraṅgamālaṃ nirantaranipatattīkṣṇakhadgavikṣiptasvahastaśastraparyastottuṅgamātaṅgamahāmahīdharasahasram bhramadbhujadaṇḍamandarābhighātaghūrṇamānasakalapattisalilasaṃghātaṃ karṇasainyasāgaraṃ nirmathya madhumathaneneva kṣīrasamudram āsāditā samaravijayalakṣmīḥ | tasya sāmprataṃ sakalamunijanaślāghanīyaḥ katham īdṛśa upaśamaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ |)

    sūtradhāraḥ

    ārye nisargasaumyam eva brāhmaṃ jyotiḥ, kuto 'pi kāraṇāt prāptavikriyam api, punaḥ svabhāva evāvatiṣṭhate | yataḥ sakalabhūpālakulapralayakālāgnirudreṇa cedipatinā samunmūlitaṃ candrānvayapārthivānāṃ pṛthivyām ādhipatyaṃ sthirīkartum ayam asya saṃrambhaḥ | paśya tathā —

  • kalpāntavātasaṃkṣobhalaṅghitāśeṣabhūbhṛtaḥ,dhairyaprasādamaryādās tā eva hi mahodadheḥ ||

    • api ca, bhagavannārāyaṇāṃśasaṃbhūtā bhūtahitāya tathāvidhapauruṣabhūṣaṇāḥ puruṣāḥ kṣitim avatīrya, niṣpāditakṛtyāḥ punaḥ śāntim eva prapadyante | tathā hi paraśurāmam evākalayatu bhavatī tāvat —

  • yena triḥsaptakṛtvo nṛpabahulavasāmāṃsamastiṣkapaṅkaprāgbhāre 'kāri bhūricyutarudhirasaridvāripūre 'bhiṣekaḥ | yasya strībālavṛddhāvadhinidhanavidhau nirdayo viśruto 'saurājanyoccāṃsakūṭatruṭanapaṭuraṭadghoradhāraḥ kuṭhāraḥ ||
  • so 'pi svavīryād avatārya bhūmer bhāraṃ samutkhāya kulaṃ nṛpāṇām,praśāntakopajvalanas tapobhiḥ śrīmān punaḥ śāmyati jāmadagnyaḥ ||

    • tathāyam api kṛtakartavyaḥ saṃprati parāṃ śāntiṃ prapannaḥ | yena ca —

  • vivekeneva nirjitya karṇaṃ moham ivorjitam,śrīkīrtivarmanṛpater bodhasyevodayaḥ kṛtaḥ ||

    • sūtradhāraḥ — ārye nisargasaumyam eva brāhmaṃ jyotiḥ, kuto 'pi kāraṇāt prāptavikriyam api, punaḥ svabhāva evāvatiṣṭhate | yataḥ sakalabhūpālakulapralayakālāgnirudreṇa cedipatinā samunmūlitaṃ candrānvayapārthivānāṃ pṛthivyām ādhipatyaṃ sthirīkartum ayam asya saṃrambhaḥ | paśya tathā —

    kalpāntavātasaṃkṣobhalaṅghitāśeṣabhūbhṛtaḥ,dhairyaprasādamaryādās tā eva hi mahodadheḥ ||

    api ca, bhagavannārāyaṇāṃśasaṃbhūtā bhūtahitāya tathāvidhapauruṣabhūṣaṇāḥ puruṣāḥ kṣitim avatīrya, niṣpāditakṛtyāḥ punaḥ śāntim eva prapadyante | tathā hi paraśurāmam evākalayatu bhavatī tāvat —

    yena triḥsaptakṛtvo nṛpabahulavasāmāṃsamastiṣkapaṅkaprāgbhāre 'kāri bhūricyutarudhirasaridvāripūre 'bhiṣekaḥ | yasya strībālavṛddhāvadhinidhanavidhau nirdayo viśruto 'saurājanyoccāṃsakūṭatruṭanapaṭuraṭadghoradhāraḥ kuṭhāraḥ ||
    so 'pi svavīryād avatārya bhūmer bhāraṃ samutkhāya kulaṃ nṛpāṇām,praśāntakopajvalanas tapobhiḥ śrīmān punaḥ śāmyati jāmadagnyaḥ ||

    tathāyam api kṛtakartavyaḥ saṃprati parāṃ śāntiṃ prapannaḥ | yena ca —

    vivekeneva nirjitya karṇaṃ moham ivorjitam,śrīkīrtivarmanṛpater bodhasyevodayaḥ kṛtaḥ ||
    ((nepathye))

    āḥ pāpa śailūṣādhama! katham, asmāsu jīvatsu, svāmino mahāmohasya vivekasakāśāt parājayam udāharasi?

    ((nepathye)) — āḥ pāpa śailūṣādhama! katham, asmāsu jīvatsu, svāmino mahāmohasya vivekasakāśāt parājayam udāharasi?

    sūtradhāraḥ

    sasaṃbhramaṃ vilokya ārye itas tāvat |

  • uttuṅgapīvarakucadvayapīḍitāṅgam,āliṅgitaḥ pulikitena bhujena ratyā,śrīmāñ jaganti madayan nayanābhirāmaḥ,kāmo 'yam eti madaghūrṇitanetrapadmaḥ ||

    • madvacanāc cāyam upajātakrodha iva lakṣyate | tad apasaraṇam evāsmākam itaḥ śreyaḥ | niṣkrāntau | prastāvanā | tataḥ praviśati yathānirdiṣṭaḥ kāmo ratiś ca |

    sūtradhāraḥ — ((sasaṃbhramaṃ vilokya)) ārye itas tāvat |

    uttuṅgapīvarakucadvayapīḍitāṅgam,āliṅgitaḥ pulikitena bhujena ratyā,śrīmāñ jaganti madayan nayanābhirāmaḥ,kāmo 'yam eti madaghūrṇitanetrapadmaḥ ||

    madvacanāc cāyam upajātakrodha iva lakṣyate | tad apasaraṇam evāsmākam itaḥ śreyaḥ | ((niṣkrāntau |)) prastāvanā | ((tataḥ praviśati yathānirdiṣṭaḥ kāmo ratiś ca |))

    kāmaḥ

    sakrodham, āḥ pāpeti pūrvoktam eva paṭhitvā nanu re re bharatādhama!

  • prabhavati manasi viveko viduṣām api śāstrasaṃbhavas tāvat,nipatanti dṛṣṭiviśikhā yāvan nendīvarākṣīṇām ||
  • api ca —
  • ramyaṃ harmyatalaṃ, navāḥ sunayanā, guñjaddvirephā latāḥ,pronmīlannavamallikā, surabhayo vātāḥ, sacandrāḥ kṣapāḥ —ity etāni jayanti hanta paritaḥ śastrāṇy amoghāni me,tad bhoḥ kīdṛg asau vivekavibhavaḥ, kīdṛg prabodhodayaḥ?

    • kāmaḥ — ((sakrodham, āḥ pāpeti pūrvoktam eva paṭhitvā)) nanu re re bharatādhama!

    prabhavati manasi viveko viduṣām api śāstrasaṃbhavas tāvat,nipatanti dṛṣṭiviśikhā yāvan nendīvarākṣīṇām ||

    api ca —

    ramyaṃ harmyatalaṃ, navāḥ sunayanā, guñjaddvirephā latāḥ,pronmīlannavamallikā, surabhayo vātāḥ, sacandrāḥ kṣapāḥ —ity etāni jayanti hanta paritaḥ śastrāṇy amoghāni me,tad bhoḥ kīdṛg asau vivekavibhavaḥ, kīdṛg prabodhodayaḥ?
    ratiḥ

    ajjaütta! garuo kkhu mahāraamahāmohassa paḍivakkho viveo tti takkemi |āryaputra! garīyān khalu mahārājamahāmohasya pratipakṣo viveka iti tarkayāmi |

    ratiḥ — ajjaütta! garuo kkhu mahāraamahāmohassa paḍivakkho viveo tti takkemi | (āryaputra! garīyān khalu mahārājamahāmohasya pratipakṣo viveka iti tarkayāmi |)

    kāmaḥ

    priye, kutas tavedaṃ strīsvabhāvasulabhaṃ vivekād bhayam utpannam? paśya —

  • api yadi viśikhāḥ śarāsanaṃ vā kusumam ayaṃ sasurāsuraṃ tathāpi,mama jagad akhilaṃ, varoru! nājñām idam atilaṅghya dhṛtiṃ muhūrtam eti ||
  • tathā hi —
  • ahalyāyā jāraḥ surapatir abhūd, ātmatanayāṃprajānātho 'yāsīd, abhajata guror indur abalām | iti prāyaḥ ko vā na padam apade 'kāryata mayā?śramo madbāṇānāṃ ka iva bhuvanonmāthavidhiṣu?

    • kāmaḥ — priye, kutas tavedaṃ strīsvabhāvasulabhaṃ vivekād bhayam utpannam? paśya —

    api yadi viśikhāḥ śarāsanaṃ vā kusumam ayaṃ sasurāsuraṃ tathāpi,mama jagad akhilaṃ, varoru! nājñām idam atilaṅghya dhṛtiṃ muhūrtam eti ||

    tathā hi —

    ahalyāyā jāraḥ surapatir abhūd, ātmatanayāṃprajānātho 'yāsīd, abhajata guror indur abalām | iti prāyaḥ ko vā na padam apade 'kāryata mayā?śramo madbāṇānāṃ ka iva bhuvanonmāthavidhiṣu?
    ratiḥ

    ajjaütta evvaṃ edaṃ | taha vi mahāsahāasaṃpaṇṇo saṅgidavvo aradī | jado 'ssa jamaṇiamappamuhā amaccā mahābalā suṇiandi |āryaputra, evaṃ etat | tathāpi mahāsahāyasaṃpannaḥ śaṅkitavyo 'ratiḥ | yato 'sya yaminiyamapramukhā amātyā mahābalāḥ śrūyante |

    ratiḥ — ajjaütta evvaṃ edaṃ | taha vi mahāsahāasaṃpaṇṇo saṅgidavvo aradī | jado 'ssa jamaṇiamappamuhā amaccā mahābalā suṇiandi | (āryaputra, evaṃ etat | tathāpi mahāsahāyasaṃpannaḥ śaṅkitavyo 'ratiḥ | yato 'sya yaminiyamapramukhā amātyā mahābalāḥ śrūyante |)

    kāmaḥ

    priye, yān etān rājño vivekasya balavato yamādīn aṣṭāv amātyān paśyasi ta ete niyatam asmābhir abhiyuktamātrād drāg eva vighaṭiṣyante | tathā hi —

  • ahiṃsā kāiva kopasya? brahmacaryādayo mama?lobhasya purataḥ ke 'mī — satyāsteyāparigrahāḥ?

    • yamaniyamāsanaprāṇāyāmapratyāhāradhyānadhāraṇāsamādhayas tu, nirvikāracittāikasādhyatvād, īṣatkarasamunmūlanā eva | api ca striya evāmīṣāṃ kṛtyās tenāite 'smadgocarā eva na vartante | yataḥ —

  • santu vilokanabhāṣaṇavilāsaparihāsakeliparirambhāḥ!smaraṇam api kāminīnām alam iha manaso vikārāya ||

    • viśeṣataś cāite madamānamātsaryadambhastambhalobhādibhir asmatsvāmivallabhair abhiyujyamānā narapatimantriṇo 'dharmam evāśrayiṣyante |

    kāmaḥ — priye, yān etān rājño vivekasya balavato yamādīn aṣṭāv amātyān paśyasi ta ete niyatam asmābhir abhiyuktamātrād drāg eva vighaṭiṣyante | tathā hi —

    ahiṃsā kāiva kopasya? brahmacaryādayo mama?lobhasya purataḥ ke 'mī — satyāsteyāparigrahāḥ?

    yamaniyamāsanaprāṇāyāmapratyāhāradhyānadhāraṇāsamādhayas tu, nirvikāracittāikasādhyatvād, īṣatkarasamunmūlanā eva | api ca striya evāmīṣāṃ kṛtyās tenāite 'smadgocarā eva na vartante | yataḥ —

    santu vilokanabhāṣaṇavilāsaparihāsakeliparirambhāḥ!smaraṇam api kāminīnām alam iha manaso vikārāya ||

    viśeṣataś cāite madamānamātsaryadambhastambhalobhādibhir asmatsvāmivallabhair abhiyujyamānā narapatimantriṇo 'dharmam evāśrayiṣyante |

    ratiḥ

    sudaṃ mae tumhāṇaṃ samadamaviveappahudīṇaṃ ca ekkaṃ uppattitthāṇaṃ ti |śrutaṃ mayā yuṣmākaṃ śamadamavivekaprabhṛtīnāṃ caikam utpattisthānam iti |

    ratiḥ — sudaṃ mae tumhāṇaṃ samadamaviveappahudīṇaṃ ca ekkaṃ uppattitthāṇaṃ ti | (śrutaṃ mayā yuṣmākaṃ śamadamavivekaprabhṛtīnāṃ caikam utpattisthānam iti |)

    kāmaḥ

    āḥ, priye, kim ucyata ekam utpattisthānam iti, nanu janaka evāsmākam abhinnaḥ | tathā hi —

  • saṃbhūtaḥ prathamamaheśvarasya saṅgān māyāyāṃ mana iti viśrutas tanūjaḥ | trailokyaṃ sakalam idaṃ visṛjya bhūyas tenātho janitam idam kuladvayaṃ naḥ ||

    • tasya ca pravṛttinivṛttī dve dharmapatnyau | tayoḥ pravṛttyāṃ samutpannaṃ mahāmohapradhānam ekaṃ kulam | nivṛttyāṃ ca dvitīyaṃ vivekapradhānam iti |

    kāmaḥ — āḥ, priye, kim ucyata ekam utpattisthānam iti, nanu janaka evāsmākam abhinnaḥ | tathā hi —

    saṃbhūtaḥ prathamamaheśvarasya saṅgān māyāyāṃ mana iti viśrutas tanūjaḥ | trailokyaṃ sakalam idaṃ visṛjya bhūyas tenātho janitam idam kuladvayaṃ naḥ ||

    tasya ca pravṛttinivṛttī dve dharmapatnyau | tayoḥ pravṛttyāṃ samutpannaṃ mahāmohapradhānam ekaṃ kulam | nivṛttyāṃ ca dvitīyaṃ vivekapradhānam iti |

    ratiḥ

    ajjaütta jaï evvaṃ, tā kiṃ ṇimittaṃ tumhāṇaṃ soarāṇaṃ vi īrisaṃ veram?āryaputra, yady evaṃ, tat kinnimittaṃ yuṣmākaṃ sodarāṇām api īdṛśaṃ vairam?

    ratiḥ — ajjaütta jaï evvaṃ, tā kiṃ ṇimittaṃ tumhāṇaṃ soarāṇaṃ vi īrisaṃ veram? (āryaputra, yady evaṃ, tat kinnimittaṃ yuṣmākaṃ sodarāṇām api īdṛśaṃ vairam?)

    kāmaḥ

    priye,

  • ekāmiṣaprabhavam eva mahīpatīnāmujjṛmbhate jagati vairam iti prasiddham | pṛthvīnimittam abhavat kurupāṇḍavānāṃtīvras tathā hi bhuvanakṣayakṛdvirodhaḥ ||

    • sarvam evāitaj jagad asmākaṃ pitryam upārjanaṃ, tac cāsmābhis tātavallabhatayā sarvam evākrāntam, teṣāṃ tu viralaḥ pracāraḥ | tenāite pāpāḥ sāṃprataṃ pitaram asmāṃś conmūlayitum udyatāḥ!

    kāmaḥ — priye,

    ekāmiṣaprabhavam eva mahīpatīnāmujjṛmbhate jagati vairam iti prasiddham | pṛthvīnimittam abhavat kurupāṇḍavānāṃtīvras tathā hi bhuvanakṣayakṛdvirodhaḥ ||

    sarvam evāitaj jagad asmākaṃ pitryam upārjanaṃ, tac cāsmābhis tātavallabhatayā sarvam evākrāntam, teṣāṃ tu viralaḥ pracāraḥ | tenāite pāpāḥ sāṃprataṃ pitaram asmāṃś conmūlayitum udyatāḥ!

    ratiḥ

    sāntaṃ pāvaṃ sāntaṃ pāvaṃ | ajjaütta kiṃ edaṃ pāvaṃ viddesamatteṇa tehiṃ āraddhaṃ? ahavā uvāo vi ko vi ettha mantido?śāntaṃ pāpaṃ, śāntaṃ pāpam! āryaputra, kiṃ etat pāpaṃ vidveṣamātreṇa tair ārabdham? athavā upāyo 'pi ko 'py atra mantritaḥ?

    ratiḥ — sāntaṃ pāvaṃ sāntaṃ pāvaṃ | ajjaütta kiṃ edaṃ pāvaṃ viddesamatteṇa tehiṃ āraddhaṃ? ahavā uvāo vi ko vi ettha mantido? (śāntaṃ pāpaṃ, śāntaṃ pāpam! āryaputra, kiṃ etat pāpaṃ vidveṣamātreṇa tair ārabdham? athavā upāyo 'pi ko 'py atra mantritaḥ?)

    kāmaḥ

    priye, asty atra kiṃcin niguḍhaṃ bījam |

    kāmaḥ — priye, asty atra kiṃcin niguḍhaṃ bījam |

    ratiḥ

    ajjaütta tā kiṃ ṇa ugghāḍīadi?āryaputra, tat kiṃ nodghāṭyate?

    ratiḥ — ajjaütta tā kiṃ ṇa ugghāḍīadi? (āryaputra, tat kiṃ nodghāṭyate?)

    kāmaḥ

    priye, bhavatī strīsvabhāvād bhīrur iti, na dāruṇakarma pāpīyasām udāhriyate!

    kāmaḥ — priye, bhavatī strīsvabhāvād bhīrur iti, na dāruṇakarma pāpīyasām udāhriyate!

    ratiḥ

    sabhayam ajjaütta kerisaṃ tam?āryaputra, kīdṛśaṃ tat?

    ratiḥ — ((sabhayam))ajjaütta kerisaṃ tam? (āryaputra, kīdṛśaṃ tat?)

    kāmaḥ

    priye, na bhetavyaṃ, na bhetavyam | hatāśānāṃ manorathamātram evāitat | asti kilāiṣā kiṃvadantī — asmākaṃ kule kālarātrikalpā vidyā nāma rākṣasī samutpatsyata iti |

    kāmaḥ — priye, na bhetavyaṃ, na bhetavyam | hatāśānāṃ manorathamātram evāitat | asti kilāiṣā kiṃvadantī — asmākaṃ kule kālarātrikalpā vidyā nāma rākṣasī samutpatsyata iti |

    ratiḥ

    sabhayam haddhi! kadhaṃ uṇa amhāṇaṃ kule rakkhasi? tti vevadi me hiaam |hā dhik! katham punar asmākaṃ kule rākṣasīti? vepate me hṛdayam |

    ratiḥ — ((sabhayam))haddhi! kadhaṃ uṇa amhāṇaṃ kule rakkhasi? tti vevadi me hiaam | (hā dhik! katham punar asmākaṃ kule rākṣasīti? vepate me hṛdayam |)

    kāmaḥ

    priye, na bhetavyaṃ, ne bhetavyaṃ | kiṃvadantīmātram etat |

    kāmaḥ — priye, na bhetavyaṃ, ne bhetavyaṃ | kiṃvadantīmātram etat |

    ratiḥ

    aha tāe rakkhasīe kiṃ kādavvam?atha tayā rākṣasyā kiṃ kartavyam?

    ratiḥ — aha tāe rakkhasīe kiṃ kādavvam? (atha tayā rākṣasyā kiṃ kartavyam?)

    kāmaḥ

    priye asti kilāiṣā prājāpatyā sarasvatī —

  • puṃsaḥ saṅgasamujjhitasya gṛhiṇī māyeti tenāpy asāvaspṛṣṭāpi manaḥ prasūya tanayaṃ; lokān asūta kramāt | tasmād eva janiṣyate punar asau vidyeti kanyā yayātātas te ca sahodarāś ca jananī sarvaṃ ca bhakṣyaṃ kulam ||

    • kāmaḥ — priye asti kilāiṣā prājāpatyā sarasvatī —

    puṃsaḥ saṅgasamujjhitasya gṛhiṇī māyeti tenāpy asāvaspṛṣṭāpi manaḥ prasūya tanayaṃ; lokān asūta kramāt | tasmād eva janiṣyate punar asau vidyeti kanyā yayātātas te ca sahodarāś ca jananī sarvaṃ ca bhakṣyaṃ kulam ||
    ratiḥ

    satrāsotkampam ˹ajjaütta! parittāāhi, parittāāhi!˼ iti bhartāram āliṅgati |(āryaputra! paritrāyasva, paritrāyasva!)

    ratiḥ — ((satrāsotkampam)) ˹ajjaütta! parittāāhi, parittāāhi!˼ ((iti bhartāram āliṅgati |))(āryaputra! paritrāyasva, paritrāyasva!)

    kāmaḥ

    sparśasukham abhinīya | svagatam |

  • sphuradromodbhedas taralataratārākuladṛśo,bhayotkampottuṅgastanayugabharāsaṅgasubhagaḥ | adhīrākṣyā guñjanmaṇivalayadorvalliracitaḥ;parīrambho modaṃ janayati ca saṃmohayati ca ||

    • prakāśam | dṛḍhaṃ pariṣvajya | priye, na bhetavyaṃ, na bhetavyam | asmāsu jīvatsu kuto vidyotpattiḥ?

    kāmaḥ — ((sparśasukham abhinīya | svagatam |))

    sphuradromodbhedas taralataratārākuladṛśo,bhayotkampottuṅgastanayugabharāsaṅgasubhagaḥ | adhīrākṣyā guñjanmaṇivalayadorvalliracitaḥ;parīrambho modaṃ janayati ca saṃmohayati ca ||

    ((prakāśam | dṛḍhaṃ pariṣvajya |)) priye, na bhetavyaṃ, na bhetavyam | asmāsu jīvatsu kuto vidyotpattiḥ?

    ratiḥ

    ajjaütta kiṃ tāe rakkhassīe uppattī amhāṇaṃ paḍivakkhāṇaṃ sammadā?āryaputra, kiṃ tasyā rākṣasyā utpattir asmākaṃ pratipakṣāṇāṃ sammatā?

    ratiḥ — ajjaütta kiṃ tāe rakkhassīe uppattī amhāṇaṃ paḍivakkhāṇaṃ sammadā? (āryaputra, kiṃ tasyā rākṣasyā utpattir asmākaṃ pratipakṣāṇāṃ sammatā?)

    kāmaḥ

    bāḍham! sā khalu vivekenopaniṣaddevyāṃ prabodhacandreṇa bhrātrā samaṃ janayitavyā | tatra sarva evāite śamadamādayaḥ pratipannodyogāḥ |

    kāmaḥ — bāḍham! sā khalu vivekenopaniṣaddevyāṃ prabodhacandreṇa bhrātrā samaṃ janayitavyā | tatra sarva evāite śamadamādayaḥ pratipannodyogāḥ |

    ratiḥ

    kahaṃ puṇa appaṇo vināsakāriṇīe vijjāe uppattī tehiṃ duvviṇīdehiṃ silāhijjaï?katham punar ātmano vināśakāriṇyā vidyāyā utpattir tair durvinītaiḥ slāghyate?

    ratiḥ — kahaṃ puṇa appaṇo vināsakāriṇīe vijjāe uppattī tehiṃ duvviṇīdehiṃ silāhijjaï? (katham punar ātmano vināśakāriṇyā vidyāyā utpattir tair durvinītaiḥ slāghyate?)

    kāmaḥ

    priye, kulakṣayapravṛttānāṃ pāpakāriṇāṃ kutaḥ svaparapratyavāyagaṇanā? paśya —

  • sahajamalinavakrabhāvabhājāṃbhavati bhavaḥ prabhavātmanāśahetuḥ | jaladharapadavīm avāpya dhūmojvalanavināśam anuprayāti nāśam ||

    • kāmaḥ — priye, kulakṣayapravṛttānāṃ pāpakāriṇāṃ kutaḥ svaparapratyavāyagaṇanā? paśya —

    sahajamalinavakrabhāvabhājāṃbhavati bhavaḥ prabhavātmanāśahetuḥ | jaladharapadavīm avāpya dhūmojvalanavināśam anuprayāti nāśam ||
    ((nepathye))

    āḥ pāpa! durātman! katham asmān eva pāpakāriṇa ity ākṣipasi | nanu re!

  • guror apy avaliptasya, kāryākāryam ajānataḥ,utpathaṃ pratipannasya, parityāgo vidhīyate ||

    • iti paurāṇikīṃ gāthāṃ purāṇavida udāharanti! anena cāsmākaṃ janakenāhaṅkārānuvartinā jagatpatiḥ pitāiva tāvad baddhaḥ! mohādibhiś ca sa eva bandhaḥ sudṛḍhatāṃ nītaḥ |

    ((nepathye)) — āḥ pāpa! durātman! katham asmān eva pāpakāriṇa ity ākṣipasi | nanu re!

    guror apy avaliptasya, kāryākāryam ajānataḥ,utpathaṃ pratipannasya, parityāgo vidhīyate ||

    iti paurāṇikīṃ gāthāṃ purāṇavida udāharanti! anena cāsmākaṃ janakenāhaṅkārānuvartinā jagatpatiḥ pitāiva tāvad baddhaḥ! mohādibhiś ca sa eva bandhaḥ sudṛḍhatāṃ nītaḥ |

    kāmaḥ

    samantād avalokya priye, ayam asmākaṃ kule jyāyān matyā devyā saha viveka ita evābhivartate | ya eṣaḥ —

  • rāgādibhiḥ svarasacāribhir āttakāntirnirbhartsyamāna iva mānadhanaḥ kṛśāṅgaḥ | matyā nitāntakaluṣīkṛtayā śaśaṅkaḥkāntyeva sāndratuhināntarito vibhāti ||

    • tan na yuktam ihāsmākam avasthātum |

    iti niṣkrāntau viṣkambhaḥ tataḥ praviśati rājā viveko matiś ca

    kāmaḥ — ((samantād avalokya)) priye, ayam asmākaṃ kule jyāyān matyā devyā saha viveka ita evābhivartate | ya eṣaḥ —

    rāgādibhiḥ svarasacāribhir āttakāntirnirbhartsyamāna iva mānadhanaḥ kṛśāṅgaḥ | matyā nitāntakaluṣīkṛtayā śaśaṅkaḥkāntyeva sāndratuhināntarito vibhāti ||

    tan na yuktam ihāsmākam avasthātum |

    ((iti niṣkrāntau)) viṣkambhaḥ ((tataḥ praviśati rājā viveko matiś ca))

    rājā

    vicintya priye, śrutaṃ tvayāsya durvinītasya kāmabaṭor madavisphūrjitaṃ vaco yad asmān eva pāpakāriṇa ity ākṣipati?

    rājā — ((vicintya)) priye, śrutaṃ tvayāsya durvinītasya kāmabaṭor madavisphūrjitaṃ vaco yad asmān eva pāpakāriṇa ity ākṣipati?

    matiḥ

    ajjaütta kiṃ appaṇo dosaṃ loo viāṇādi?āryaputra, kim ātmano doṣaṃ loko vijānāti?

    matiḥ — ajjaütta kiṃ appaṇo dosaṃ loo viāṇādi? (āryaputra, kim ātmano doṣaṃ loko vijānāti?)

    rājā

    paśya —_

  • asāv ahaṅkāraparair durātmabhirnibadhya taiḥ pāpaśaṭhair madādibhiḥ,ciraṃ cidānandamayo nirañjanojagatpatir dīnadaśām anīyata ||

    • ta ete puṇyakāriṇo vayaṃ tu tanmuktaye pravṛttāḥ pāpakāriṇa! ity aho jitaṃ durātmabhiḥ!

    rājā — paśya —_

    asāv ahaṅkāraparair durātmabhirnibadhya taiḥ pāpaśaṭhair madādibhiḥ,ciraṃ cidānandamayo nirañjanojagatpatir dīnadaśām anīyata ||

    ta ete puṇyakāriṇo vayaṃ tu tanmuktaye pravṛttāḥ pāpakāriṇa! ity aho jitaṃ durātmabhiḥ!

    matiḥ

    ajjaütta, jado so sahaāṇandasundarasahāvo ṇiccappaāsapphurantasaalattihuaṇappaāro paramessaro suṇīadi | tā kahaṃ edehiṃ duvviṇoḍhḍhehiṃ baṃdhia mahāmohasāare ṇikkhitto?āryaputra, yato 'sau sahajānandasundarasvabhāvo nityaprakāśasphuratsakalatribhuvanapracāraḥ parameśvaraḥ śrūyate | tasmāt katham etair dirvidagdhair bandhitvā mahāmohasāgare nikṣiptaḥ |

    matiḥ — ajjaütta, jado so sahaāṇandasundarasahāvo ṇiccappaāsapphurantasaalattihuaṇappaāro paramessaro suṇīadi | tā kahaṃ edehiṃ duvviṇoḍhḍhehiṃ baṃdhia mahāmohasāare ṇikkhitto? (āryaputra, yato 'sau sahajānandasundarasvabhāvo nityaprakāśasphuratsakalatribhuvanapracāraḥ parameśvaraḥ śrūyate | tasmāt katham etair dirvidagdhair bandhitvā mahāmohasāgare nikṣiptaḥ |)

    rājā

    priye,

  • satatadhṛtir apy uccaiḥ śānto 'py avāptamahodayo'py adhigatanayo 'py antaḥsvaccho 'py udīritadhīr api,tyajati sahajaṃ dhairyaṃ strībhiḥ pratāritamānasaḥ | svam api yad ayaṃ māyāsaṅgāt pumān iti vismṛtaḥ?

    • rājā — priye,

    satatadhṛtir apy uccaiḥ śānto 'py avāptamahodayo'py adhigatanayo 'py antaḥsvaccho 'py udīritadhīr api,tyajati sahajaṃ dhairyaṃ strībhiḥ pratāritamānasaḥ | svam api yad ayaṃ māyāsaṅgāt pumān iti vismṛtaḥ?
    matiḥ

    ajjaütta, ṇaṃ andhakāralehāe sahassarassiṇo tirakkāro jaṃ māāe taha papphurantamahappaāsasāarassa devassa vi ahihavo |āryaputra, nanu andhakāralekhayā sahasraraśmes tiraskāro yan māyayā tathā prasphuranmahāprakāśasāgarasya devasyāpy abhibhavaḥ |

    matiḥ — ajjaütta, ṇaṃ andhakāralehāe sahassarassiṇo tirakkāro jaṃ māāe taha papphurantamahappaāsasāarassa devassa vi ahihavo | (āryaputra, nanu andhakāralekhayā sahasraraśmes tiraskāro yan māyayā tathā prasphuranmahāprakāśasāgarasya devasyāpy abhibhavaḥ |)

    rājā

    priye, avicārasiddheyaṃ veśyāvilāsinīva māyā asato 'pi bhāvānupadarśayantī puruṣaṃ vañcayati | paśya —

  • sphaṭikamaṇivad bhāsvān devaḥ pragāḍham anāryayāvikṛtim anayā nītaḥ kām apy asaṅgatavikriyaḥ | na khalu tad upaśleṣād asya vyapaiti rucir manāk,prabhavati tathā 'py eṣā puṃso vidhātum adhīratām ||

    • rājā — priye, avicārasiddheyaṃ veśyāvilāsinīva māyā asato 'pi bhāvānupadarśayantī puruṣaṃ vañcayati | paśya —

    sphaṭikamaṇivad bhāsvān devaḥ pragāḍham anāryayāvikṛtim anayā nītaḥ kām apy asaṅgatavikriyaḥ | na khalu tad upaśleṣād asya vyapaiti rucir manāk,prabhavati tathā 'py eṣā puṃso vidhātum adhīratām ||
    matiḥ

    ajjaütta, kiṃ puṇa kālaṇaṃ jeṇa taha udāracaridaṃ duvviḍhḍhā patāredi?āryaputra, kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ yena sā tathodāracaritaṃ durvidagdhā pratārayati?

    matiḥ — ajjaütta, kiṃ puṇa kālaṇaṃ jeṇa taha udāracaridaṃ duvviḍhḍhā patāredi? (āryaputra, kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ yena sā tathodāracaritaṃ durvidagdhā pratārayati?)

    rājā

    na khalu prayojanaṃ kāraṇaṃ vā vilokya māyā pravartate | svabhāvaḥ khalv asau strīpiśācīnāṃ | paśya —

  • saṃmohayanti, madayanti, viḍambayanti;nirbhartsayanti, ramayanti, viṣādayanti | etāḥ praviśya sadayaṃ hṛdayaṃ narāṇāṃ,kiṃ nāma vāmanayanā na samācaranti?

    • asti cāparam api kāraṇam |

    rājā — na khalu prayojanaṃ kāraṇaṃ vā vilokya māyā pravartate | svabhāvaḥ khalv asau strīpiśācīnāṃ | paśya —

    saṃmohayanti, madayanti, viḍambayanti;nirbhartsayanti, ramayanti, viṣādayanti | etāḥ praviśya sadayaṃ hṛdayaṃ narāṇāṃ,kiṃ nāma vāmanayanā na samācaranti?

    asti cāparam api kāraṇam |

    matiḥ

    ajjaütta, kiṃ ṇāma taṃ kālaṇam?āryaputra, kiṃ nāma tat kāraṇam |

    matiḥ — ajjaütta, kiṃ ṇāma taṃ kālaṇam? (āryaputra, kiṃ nāma tat kāraṇam |)

    rājā

    evam anayā durācārayā vicintitaṃ yad ahaṃ tāvad gatayauvanā varṣīyasījātā | ayaṃ ca purāṇapuruṣaḥ svabhāvād eva viṣayarasavimukhaḥ | tataḥ svatanayam eva pārameśvarapade niveśayāmīti tam eva mātur abhiprāyam āsādya nitāntatatpratyāsannatayā tadrūpatām ivāpannena manasā navadvārāṇi purāṇi racayitvā |

  • eko 'pi bahudhā teṣu vicchidyeva niveśitaḥ | svaceṣṭitam atho tasmin nidadhāti maṇāv iva ||

    • rājā — evam anayā durācārayā vicintitaṃ yad ahaṃ tāvad gatayauvanā varṣīyasījātā | ayaṃ ca purāṇapuruṣaḥ svabhāvād eva viṣayarasavimukhaḥ | tataḥ svatanayam eva pārameśvarapade niveśayāmīti tam eva mātur abhiprāyam āsādya nitāntatatpratyāsannatayā tadrūpatām ivāpannena manasā navadvārāṇi purāṇi racayitvā |

    eko 'pi bahudhā teṣu vicchidyeva niveśitaḥ | svaceṣṭitam atho tasmin nidadhāti maṇāv iva ||
    matiḥ

    vicintya jārisī mādā putto vi tāriso jevva jādo |yādṛśī mātā putro 'pi tāḍṛśa eva jātaḥ |

    matiḥ — ((vicintya))jārisī mādā putto vi tāriso jevva jādo | (yādṛśī mātā putro 'pi tāḍṛśa eva jātaḥ |)

    rājā

    tato 'sāv ahaṃkāreṇa cittasya jyeṣṭhaputreṇa naptrā pariṣvaktaḥ | tataś cāsāv īśvaraḥ —

  • «jāto 'haṃ janako mamāiṣa jananī kṣetraṃ kalatraṃ kulaṃputrā mitram arātayo vasu balaṃ vidyāḥ suhṛd bāndhavāḥ» | cittaspanditakalpanām anubhavan vidvān avidyāmayīṃnidrām etya vighūrṇito bahuvidhān svapnān imān paśyati ||

    • rājā — tato 'sāv ahaṃkāreṇa cittasya jyeṣṭhaputreṇa naptrā pariṣvaktaḥ | tataś cāsāv īśvaraḥ —

    «jāto 'haṃ janako mamāiṣa jananī kṣetraṃ kalatraṃ kulaṃputrā mitram arātayo vasu balaṃ vidyāḥ suhṛd bāndhavāḥ» | cittaspanditakalpanām anubhavan vidvān avidyāmayīṃnidrām etya vighūrṇito bahuvidhān svapnān imān paśyati ||
    matiḥ

    ajjaütta evvaṃ dīhadīhataraṇiddāviddāviappabohe paramessare kahaṃ pabohuppattī bhavissadi?āryaputra, evaṃ dīrghadīrghataranidrāvidrāvitaprabodhe parameśvare kathaṃ prabodhotpattir bhaviṣyati |

    matiḥ — ajjaütta evvaṃ dīhadīhataraṇiddāviddāviappabohe paramessare kahaṃ pabohuppattī bhavissadi? (āryaputra, evaṃ dīrghadīrghataranidrāvidrāvitaprabodhe parameśvare kathaṃ prabodhotpattir bhaviṣyati |)

    rājā

    salajjam adhomukhas tiṣṭhati |

    rājā — ((salajjam adhomukhas tiṣṭhati |))

    matiḥ

    kitti guruaralajjābharaṇamidaseharo tūṇhīṃbhūdo 'si?kimiti gurutaralajjābharanamitaśekharas tūṣṇīṃbhūto 'si |

    matiḥ — kitti guruaralajjābharaṇamidaseharo tūṇhīṃbhūdo 'si? (kimiti gurutaralajjābharanamitaśekharas tūṣṇīṃbhūto 'si |)

    rājā

    priye, serṣyaṃ prāyeṇa yoṣitāṃ bhavati hṛdayam | tena sāparāḍham ivātmānaṃ śaṅke |

    rājā — priye, serṣyaṃ prāyeṇa yoṣitāṃ bhavati hṛdayam | tena sāparāḍham ivātmānaṃ śaṅke |

    matiḥ

    aṇṇāo tāo itthiāo, jāo sarasappaüttassa vā dhammapahavāvārappavuttassa vā bhattuṇo hiaadiaṃ vihaṇandi |anyās tāḥ striyo, yāḥ svarasapravṛttasya vā dharmapathavyāpārapravṛttasya vā bhartur hṛdayepsitaṃ vighnanti |

    matiḥ — aṇṇāo tāo itthiāo, jāo sarasappaüttassa vā dhammapahavāvārappavuttassa vā bhattuṇo hiaadiaṃ vihaṇandi | (anyās tāḥ striyo, yāḥ svarasapravṛttasya vā dharmapathavyāpārapravṛttasya vā bhartur hṛdayepsitaṃ vighnanti |)

    rājā

    priye —_

  • māninyāś ciraviprayogajanitāsūyākulāyā bhavecchāntyāder anukūlanād upaniṣaddevyā mayā saṃgamaḥ,tūṣṇīṃ ced viṣayānapāsya bhavatī tiṣṭhen muhūrtaṃ tatojāgratsvapnasuṣuptidhāmavirahāt prāptaḥ prabodhodayaḥ ||

    • rājā — priye —_

    māninyāś ciraviprayogajanitāsūyākulāyā bhavecchāntyāder anukūlanād upaniṣaddevyā mayā saṃgamaḥ,tūṣṇīṃ ced viṣayānapāsya bhavatī tiṣṭhen muhūrtaṃ tatojāgratsvapnasuṣuptidhāmavirahāt prāptaḥ prabodhodayaḥ ||
    matiḥ

    ajjaütta, jadi evaṃ kulappahuṇo diḍhagaṃthiṇiṭṭhāvia bandhamokkho bhodi tado tāe ṇiccāṇubaddho jevva ajjaütto bhodu! suṭṭhu me piam |āryaputra, yady evaṃ kulaprabhor dṛḍhagranthiniṣṭhāpita bandhamokṣo bhavati tatas tayā nityānubaddha evāryaputro bhavatu | suṣṭhu me priyam |

    matiḥ — ajjaütta, jadi evaṃ kulappahuṇo diḍhagaṃthiṇiṭṭhāvia bandhamokkho bhodi tado tāe ṇiccāṇubaddho jevva ajjaütto bhodu! suṭṭhu me piam | (āryaputra, yady evaṃ kulaprabhor dṛḍhagranthiniṣṭhāpita bandhamokṣo bhavati tatas tayā nityānubaddha evāryaputro bhavatu | suṣṭhu me priyam |)

    rājā

    yady evaṃ prasannāsi siddhās tarhy asmākaṃ manorathāḥ | tathā hi —

  • baddhvāiko bahudhā vibhajya jagatām ādiḥ prabhuḥ śāśvataḥkṣiptvā yaiḥ puruṣaḥ pureṣu paramo mṛtyoḥ padaṃ prāpitaḥ | teṣāṃ brahmabhidāṃ vidhāya vidhivat prāṇāntikaṃ vidyayāprāyaścittam idaṃ mayā punar asau brahmāikatāṃ nīyate ||

    • tad bhavatu | prastutavidhānāya śamādīn udyojayāmaḥ | niṣkrāntau iti śrīkṛṣṇamiśrayatiracite prabodhacandrodaye māyāvilasitaṃ nāma prathamo 'ṅkaḥ |

    rājā — yady evaṃ prasannāsi siddhās tarhy asmākaṃ manorathāḥ | tathā hi —

    baddhvāiko bahudhā vibhajya jagatām ādiḥ prabhuḥ śāśvataḥkṣiptvā yaiḥ puruṣaḥ pureṣu paramo mṛtyoḥ padaṃ prāpitaḥ | teṣāṃ brahmabhidāṃ vidhāya vidhivat prāṇāntikaṃ vidyayāprāyaścittam idaṃ mayā punar asau brahmāikatāṃ nīyate ||

    tad bhavatu | prastutavidhānāya śamādīn udyojayāmaḥ | ((niṣkrāntau)) iti śrīkṛṣṇamiśrayatiracite prabodhacandrodaye māyāvilasitaṃ nāma prathamo 'ṅkaḥ |

    § 2

    p.2, l.1

    (p.2, l.1)tataḥ praviśati dambhaḥ |

    ((tataḥ praviśati dambhaḥ |))

    dambhaḥ

    ādiṣṭo 'smi mahārājamahāmohena yathā — vatsa dambha pratijñātaṃ sāmātyena vivekena prabodhodayāya, preṣitāś ca teṣu teṣu tīrtheṣu śamadamādayaḥ | sa cāyam asmākam upasthitaḥ kulakṣayo, bhavadbhir avahitaiḥ pratikartavyaḥ | tatra pṛthivyāṃ paramaṃ muktikṣetraṃ vārāṇasī nāma nagarī | tad bhavāṃs tatra gatvā caturṇām apy āśramāṇāṃ niḥśreyasavighnāya prayatatāṃ iti | tad idānīṃ vaśīkṛtabhūyiṣṭhā mayā vārāṇasī saṃpāditaś ca svāmino yathānirdiṣṭa ādeśaḥ | tathā hi madadhiṣṭhitair idānīm —

  • veśyāveśmasu sīdhugandhilalanāvaktrāsavāmoditairnītvā nirbharamanmathotsavarasair unnidracandrāḥ kṣapāḥ,sarvajñā iti dīkṣitā iti cirāt prāptāgnihotrā itibrahmajñā iti tāpasā iti divā dhūrtair jagad vañcyate ||

    • vilokya ko 'py ayaṃ pāntho bhāgīrathīm uttīrya sāṃpratam ita evābhivartate? yathā cāyaṃ —

  • jvalann ivābhimānena, grasann iva jagattrayīm,bhartsayann iva vāgjālaiḥ, prajñayopahasann iva ||

    • tathā tarkayāmi | nūnam ayaṃ dakṣiṇarāḍhāpradeśād āgataḥ | tad asmād āryasyāhaṃkārasya vṛttāntam avagacchāmi | iti parikrāmati | tataḥ praviśaty ahaṅkāro yathānirdiṣṭaḥ |

    dambhaḥ — ādiṣṭo 'smi mahārājamahāmohena yathā — vatsa dambha pratijñātaṃ sāmātyena vivekena prabodhodayāya, preṣitāś ca teṣu teṣu tīrtheṣu śamadamādayaḥ | sa cāyam asmākam upasthitaḥ kulakṣayo, bhavadbhir avahitaiḥ pratikartavyaḥ | tatra pṛthivyāṃ paramaṃ muktikṣetraṃ vārāṇasī nāma nagarī | tad bhavāṃs tatra gatvā caturṇām apy āśramāṇāṃ niḥśreyasavighnāya prayatatāṃ iti | tad idānīṃ vaśīkṛtabhūyiṣṭhā mayā vārāṇasī saṃpāditaś ca svāmino yathānirdiṣṭa ādeśaḥ | tathā hi madadhiṣṭhitair idānīm —

    veśyāveśmasu sīdhugandhilalanāvaktrāsavāmoditairnītvā nirbharamanmathotsavarasair unnidracandrāḥ kṣapāḥ,sarvajñā iti dīkṣitā iti cirāt prāptāgnihotrā itibrahmajñā iti tāpasā iti divā dhūrtair jagad vañcyate ||

    ((vilokya)) ko 'py ayaṃ pāntho bhāgīrathīm uttīrya sāṃpratam ita evābhivartate? yathā cāyaṃ —

    jvalann ivābhimānena, grasann iva jagattrayīm,bhartsayann iva vāgjālaiḥ, prajñayopahasann iva ||

    tathā tarkayāmi | nūnam ayaṃ dakṣiṇarāḍhāpradeśād āgataḥ | tad asmād āryasyāhaṃkārasya vṛttāntam avagacchāmi | ((iti parikrāmati |)) ((tataḥ praviśaty ahaṅkāro yathānirdiṣṭaḥ |))

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    aho! mūrkhabahulaṃ jagat! tathā hi —

  • nāivāśrāvi guror mataṃ, na viditaṃ kaumārilaṃ darśanaṃ,tattvajñānam aho na śālikagirāṃ vācaspateḥ kā kathā?sūktaṃ nāpi mahōdadher adhigataṃ, māhāvratī nekṣitā,sūkṣmā vastuvicāraṇā, nṛpaśubhiḥ svasthaiḥ kathaṃ sthīyate ||

    • vilokya ete tāvad arthāvadhāraṇavidhurāḥ; svādhyāyādhyayanamātraniratā vedaviplāvakā eva | punar anyato gatvā | ete ca bhikṣāmātraṃ gṛhītayativratā, muṇḍitamuṇḍāḥ paṇḍitammanyā vedāntaśāstraṃ vyākulayanti | vihasya

  • pratyakṣādipramāsiddhaviruddhārthābhidhāyinaḥ,vedāntā yadi śāstrāṇi bauddhaiḥ kim aparādhyate?

    • tad etad vāṅmātraśravaṇam api gurutaraduritodayāya! punar anyato gatvā | ete ca śaivapāśupatādayo durabhyastākṣapādamatāḥ paśavaḥ pāṣaṇḍāḥ! amīṣāṃ saṃbhāṣaṇād api narā narakaṃ yānti | tad ete darśanapathād dūrataḥ pariharaṇīyāḥ | punar anyato gatvā | ete ca —

  • gaṅgātīrataraṅgaśītalaśilāvinyastabhāsvadbṛsīsaṃviṣṭāḥ, kuśamuṣṭimaṇḍitamahādaṇḍāḥ karaṇḍojjvalāḥ,paryāyagrathitākṣasūtravalayapratyekabījagrahavyagrāgrāṅgulayo haranti dhanināṃ vittāny, aho dāmbhikāḥ!

    • anyato gatvā vilokya | ete tridaṇḍavyapadeśajīvino dvaitādvaitamārgaparibhraṣṭā eva! aye! kasyāitad dvāropāntanikhātātiprāṃśuvaṃśakāṇḍatāṇḍavitadhautasitasūkṣmāmbarasahasram, itas tato vinyastakṛṣṇājinadṛṣadupalasamiccaṣālolūkhalamusalam, anavaratahutājyagandhīdhūmaśyāmalitagaganamaṇḍalam amarasarito nātidūre vibhāty āśramamaṇḍalam? nūnam idaṃ kasyāpi gṛhamedhino gṛhaṃ bhaviṣyati | bhavatu, yuktam asmākam atipavitram etad dvitridivasanivāsasthānam | praveśaṃ nāṭayati vilokya ca | aye!

  • mṛdbindulāñchitalalāṭabhujodaroraḥkāṇṭh'oṣṭhapṛṣṭhacibukorukapolajānuḥ;cūḍāgrakarṇakaṭipāṇivirājamānadarbhāṅkuraḥ — sphurati! mūrta ivāiṣa dambhaḥ ||

    • bhavatūpasarpāmy enam | upasṛtya | kalyāṇam bhavatu, bhavatām! dambho huṃkāreṇa nivārayati | praviśati baṭuḥ |

    ahaṅkāraḥ — aho! mūrkhabahulaṃ jagat! tathā hi —

    nāivāśrāvi guror mataṃ, na viditaṃ kaumārilaṃ darśanaṃ,tattvajñānam aho na śālikagirāṃ vācaspateḥ kā kathā?sūktaṃ nāpi mahōdadher adhigataṃ, māhāvratī nekṣitā,sūkṣmā vastuvicāraṇā, nṛpaśubhiḥ svasthaiḥ kathaṃ sthīyate ||

    ((vilokya)) ete tāvad arthāvadhāraṇavidhurāḥ; svādhyāyādhyayanamātraniratā vedaviplāvakā eva | ((punar anyato gatvā |)) ete ca bhikṣāmātraṃ gṛhītayativratā, muṇḍitamuṇḍāḥ paṇḍitammanyā vedāntaśāstraṃ vyākulayanti | ((vihasya))

    pratyakṣādipramāsiddhaviruddhārthābhidhāyinaḥ,vedāntā yadi śāstrāṇi bauddhaiḥ kim aparādhyate?

    tad etad vāṅmātraśravaṇam api gurutaraduritodayāya! ((punar anyato gatvā |)) ete ca śaivapāśupatādayo durabhyastākṣapādamatāḥ paśavaḥ pāṣaṇḍāḥ! amīṣāṃ saṃbhāṣaṇād api narā narakaṃ yānti | tad ete darśanapathād dūrataḥ pariharaṇīyāḥ | ((punar anyato gatvā |)) ete ca —

    gaṅgātīrataraṅgaśītalaśilāvinyastabhāsvadbṛsīsaṃviṣṭāḥ, kuśamuṣṭimaṇḍitamahādaṇḍāḥ karaṇḍojjvalāḥ,paryāyagrathitākṣasūtravalayapratyekabījagrahavyagrāgrāṅgulayo haranti dhanināṃ vittāny, aho dāmbhikāḥ!

    ((anyato gatvā vilokya |)) ete tridaṇḍavyapadeśajīvino dvaitādvaitamārgaparibhraṣṭā eva! aye! kasyāitad dvāropāntanikhātātiprāṃśuvaṃśakāṇḍatāṇḍavitadhautasitasūkṣmāmbarasahasram, itas tato vinyastakṛṣṇājinadṛṣadupalasamiccaṣālolūkhalamusalam, anavaratahutājyagandhīdhūmaśyāmalitagaganamaṇḍalam amarasarito nātidūre vibhāty āśramamaṇḍalam? nūnam idaṃ kasyāpi gṛhamedhino gṛhaṃ bhaviṣyati | bhavatu, yuktam asmākam atipavitram etad dvitridivasanivāsasthānam | ((praveśaṃ nāṭayati vilokya ca |)) aye!

    mṛdbindulāñchitalalāṭabhujodaroraḥkāṇṭh'oṣṭhapṛṣṭhacibukorukapolajānuḥ;cūḍāgrakarṇakaṭipāṇivirājamānadarbhāṅkuraḥ — sphurati! mūrta ivāiṣa dambhaḥ ||

    bhavatūpasarpāmy enam | ((upasṛtya |)) kalyāṇam bhavatu, bhavatām! ((dambho huṃkāreṇa nivārayati |)) ((praviśati baṭuḥ |))

    baṭuḥ

    sasaṃbhramam | brahman, dūrata eva sthīyatām! yataḥ pādau prakṣālya etad āśramapadaṃ praveṣṭavyam!

    baṭuḥ — ((sasaṃbhramam |)) brahman, dūrata eva sthīyatām! yataḥ pādau prakṣālya etad āśramapadaṃ praveṣṭavyam!

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    sakrodham āḥ pāpa! turuṣkadeśaṃ prāptāḥ smaḥ, yatra śrotriyān atithīn āsanapādyādibhir api gṛhiṇo nopatiṣṭhanti!

    ahaṅkāraḥ — ((sakrodham)) āḥ pāpa! turuṣkadeśaṃ prāptāḥ smaḥ, yatra śrotriyān atithīn āsanapādyādibhir api gṛhiṇo nopatiṣṭhanti!

    dambhaḥ

    hastasaṃjñayā samāśvāsayati |

    dambhaḥ — ((hastasaṃjñayā samāśvāsayati |))

    baṭuḥ

    evam ārādhyapādā ājñāpayanti dūradeśād āgatasyāryasya kulaśīlādikaṃ na samyag asmābhir viditam |

    baṭuḥ — evam ārādhyapādā ājñāpayanti dūradeśād āgatasyāryasya kulaśīlādikaṃ na samyag asmābhir viditam |

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    āḥ! katham asmākam api kulaśīlādikam idānīṃ parīkṣitavyam? śrūyatām!

  • gauḍaṃ rāṣṭram anuttamaṃ, nirūpamā tatrāpi rāḍhāpurī,bhūriśreṣṭhikanāma dhāma paramaṃ tatrottamo naḥ pitā | tatputrāś ca mahākulā na viditāḥ kasyātra teṣām api,prajñāśīlavivekadhairyavinayācārair ahaṃ cottamaḥ

    • dambho baṭuṃ paśyati |

    ahaṅkāraḥ — āḥ! katham asmākam api kulaśīlādikam idānīṃ parīkṣitavyam? śrūyatām!

    gauḍaṃ rāṣṭram anuttamaṃ, nirūpamā tatrāpi rāḍhāpurī,bhūriśreṣṭhikanāma dhāma paramaṃ tatrottamo naḥ pitā | tatputrāś ca mahākulā na viditāḥ kasyātra teṣām api,prajñāśīlavivekadhairyavinayācārair ahaṃ cottamaḥ

    ((dambho baṭuṃ paśyati |))

    baṭuḥ

    tāmraghaṭīṃ gṛhītvā | brahman! pādaśaucaṃ vidhīyatām!

    baṭuḥ — ((tāmraghaṭīṃ gṛhītvā |)) brahman! pādaśaucaṃ vidhīyatām!

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    bhavatu | ko 'tra virodhaḥ? evaṃ kriyate | tathā kṛtvopasarpati dambho dantān saṃpīḍya baṭuṃ paśyati

    ahaṅkāraḥ — bhavatu | ko 'tra virodhaḥ? evaṃ kriyate | ((tathā kṛtvopasarpati)) ((dambho dantān saṃpīḍya baṭuṃ paśyati))

    baṭuḥ

    dūre tāvat sthīyatām! vātāhatāḥ prasvedakaṇikāḥ prasaranti!

    baṭuḥ — dūre tāvat sthīyatām! vātāhatāḥ prasvedakaṇikāḥ prasaranti!

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    aho! apūrvaṃ idaṃ brāhmaṇyam!

    ahaṅkāraḥ — aho! apūrvaṃ idaṃ brāhmaṇyam!

    baṭuḥ

    brahman evam etat! tathā hi —

  • aspṛṣṭacaraṇā hy asya cūḍāmaṇimarīcibhiḥ,nīrājayanti bhūpālāḥ pādapīṭhāntabhūtalam ||

    • baṭuḥ — brahman evam etat! tathā hi —

    aspṛṣṭacaraṇā hy asya cūḍāmaṇimarīcibhiḥ,nīrājayanti bhūpālāḥ pādapīṭhāntabhūtalam ||
    ahaṅkāraḥ

    svagatam | aye! dambhagrāhyo 'yaṃ deśaḥ! prakāśam bhavatu | asminn āsane upaviśāmi! tathā kartum icchati |

    ahaṅkāraḥ — ((svagatam |)) aye! dambhagrāhyo 'yaṃ deśaḥ! ((prakāśam)) bhavatu | asminn āsane upaviśāmi! ((tathā kartum icchati |))

    baṭuḥ

    māivam! nārādhyapādānām anyair āsanam ākramyate!

    baṭuḥ — māivam! nārādhyapādānām anyair āsanam ākramyate!

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    āḥ pāpa! asmābhir api dakṣiṇarāḍhāpradeśaprasiddhaviśuddhibhir nākramaṇīyam idam āsanam! śṛṇu re mūrkha —

  • nāsmākaṃ jananī tathojjvalakulā, sacchrotriyāṇāṃ punarvyūḍhā kācana kanyakā khalu mayā tenāsmi tātādhikaḥ | asmatsyālakabhāgineyadayitā mithyābhiśastā, yatastatsaṃparkavaśān mayā svagṛhiṇī preyasy api projjhitā ||

    • ahaṅkāraḥ — āḥ pāpa! asmābhir api dakṣiṇarāḍhāpradeśaprasiddhaviśuddhibhir nākramaṇīyam idam āsanam! śṛṇu re mūrkha —

    nāsmākaṃ jananī tathojjvalakulā, sacchrotriyāṇāṃ punarvyūḍhā kācana kanyakā khalu mayā tenāsmi tātādhikaḥ | asmatsyālakabhāgineyadayitā mithyābhiśastā, yatastatsaṃparkavaśān mayā svagṛhiṇī preyasy api projjhitā ||
    dambhaḥ

    brahman, yady apy evaṃ, tathāpy aviditāsmadvṛttānto bhavān | tathā hi —

  • sadanam upagato 'haṃ pūrvam ambhojayoneḥ,sapadi munibhir uccair āsaneṣūjjhiteṣu,saśapatham anunīya brahmaṇā gomayāmbhaḥparimṛjitanijorāv āśu saṃveśito 'smi ||

    • dambhaḥ — brahman, yady apy evaṃ, tathāpy aviditāsmadvṛttānto bhavān | tathā hi —

    sadanam upagato 'haṃ pūrvam ambhojayoneḥ,sapadi munibhir uccair āsaneṣūjjhiteṣu,saśapatham anunīya brahmaṇā gomayāmbhaḥparimṛjitanijorāv āśu saṃveśito 'smi ||
    ahaṅkāraḥ

    svagatam aho! dāmbhikasya brāḥmaṇasyātyuktiḥ! vicintya athavā … dambhasyāiva! bhavatv evaṃ tāvat! prakāśam āḥ, kim evaṃ garvāyase? sakrodham

  • are! ka iva vāsavaḥ? kathaya ko nu padmodbhavo?vada prabhavabhūmayo jagati kā ṛṣīṇām api?avehi tapaso balaṃ mama purandarāṇāṃ śataṃśataṃ ca parameṣṭhināṃ patatu vā munīnāṃ śatam ||

    • ahaṅkāraḥ — ((svagatam)) aho! dāmbhikasya brāḥmaṇasyātyuktiḥ! ((vicintya)) athavā … dambhasyāiva! bhavatv evaṃ tāvat! ((prakāśam)) āḥ, kim evaṃ garvāyase? ((sakrodham))

    are! ka iva vāsavaḥ? kathaya ko nu padmodbhavo?vada prabhavabhūmayo jagati kā ṛṣīṇām api?avehi tapaso balaṃ mama purandarāṇāṃ śataṃśataṃ ca parameṣṭhināṃ patatu vā munīnāṃ śatam ||
    dambhaḥ

    vilokya sānandam | aye! āryaḥ pitāmaho 'asmākam ahaṅkāraḥ! ārya! dambho lobhātmajo 'haṃ bho abhivādaye!

    dambhaḥ — ((vilokya sānandam |)) aye! āryaḥ pitāmaho 'asmākam ahaṅkāraḥ! ārya! dambho lobhātmajo 'haṃ bho abhivādaye!

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    vatsa, āyuṣmān bhava! bālaḥ khalv asi mayā dvāparānte dṛṣṭaḥ! saṃprati cirakālaviprakarṣād vārdhakyagrastatayā ca na samyak pratyabhijānāmi! api tvatkumārasyānṛtasya kuśalam?

    ahaṅkāraḥ — vatsa, āyuṣmān bhava! bālaḥ khalv asi mayā dvāparānte dṛṣṭaḥ! saṃprati cirakālaviprakarṣād vārdhakyagrastatayā ca na samyak pratyabhijānāmi! api tvatkumārasyānṛtasya kuśalam?

    dambhaḥ

    atha kim? so 'py atrāiva, mahāmohasyājñayā vartate | na hi tena vinā mūhurtam apy ahaṃ prabhavāmi |

    dambhaḥ — atha kim? so 'py atrāiva, mahāmohasyājñayā vartate | na hi tena vinā mūhurtam apy ahaṃ prabhavāmi |

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    atha tava mātāpitarau tṛṣṇālobhāv api kuśalau?

    ahaṅkāraḥ — atha tava mātāpitarau tṛṣṇālobhāv api kuśalau?

    dambhaḥ

    tāv api rājño mahāmohasyājñayā 'trāiva vartete | tayor vinā, kṣaṇam api na tiṣṭhāmi | āryamiśraiḥ punaḥ kena prayojanenātra prasādaḥ kṛtaḥ?

    dambhaḥ — tāv api rājño mahāmohasyājñayā 'trāiva vartete | tayor vinā, kṣaṇam api na tiṣṭhāmi | āryamiśraiḥ punaḥ kena prayojanenātra prasādaḥ kṛtaḥ?

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    vatsa, mayā mahāmohasya vivekasakāśād atyāhitaṃ śrutam | tena tad vṛttāntaṃ pratyetum āgato 'smi |

    ahaṅkāraḥ — vatsa, mayā mahāmohasya vivekasakāśād atyāhitaṃ śrutam | tena tad vṛttāntaṃ pratyetum āgato 'smi |

    dambhaḥ

    tarhi svāgatam evāryasya | yato mahārājasyāpīndralokād atrāgamanaṃ śrūyate | asti ca kiṃvadantī yad devena vārāṇasī rājadhānī vastuṃ nirūpiteti |

    dambhaḥ — tarhi svāgatam evāryasya | yato mahārājasyāpīndralokād atrāgamanaṃ śrūyate | asti ca kiṃvadantī yad devena vārāṇasī rājadhānī vastuṃ nirūpiteti |

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    kiṃ punar vārāṇasyāṃ sarvātmanā mohasyāvasthānakāraṇam iti?

    ahaṅkāraḥ — kiṃ punar vārāṇasyāṃ sarvātmanā mohasyāvasthānakāraṇam iti?

    dambhaḥ

    ārya, nanu vivekoparodha eva | tathā hi —

  • vidyāprabodhodayajanmabhūmir, vārāṇasī brahmapurī duratyayā | asau kulocchedavidhiṃ cikitsur, nirvastum atrecchati nityam eva ||

    • dambhaḥ — ārya, nanu vivekoparodha eva | tathā hi —

    vidyāprabodhodayajanmabhūmir, vārāṇasī brahmapurī duratyayā | asau kulocchedavidhiṃ cikitsur, nirvastum atrecchati nityam eva ||
    ahaṅkāraḥ

    sabhayam yady evam, aśakyapratīkāra evāyam arthaḥ | yataḥ —

  • paramam aviduṣāṃ padaṃ narāṇāṃpuravijayī karuṇāvidheyacetāḥkathayati bhagavān ihāntakāle,bhavabhayakātaratārakaṃ prabodham ||

    • ahaṅkāraḥ — ((sabhayam)) yady evam, aśakyapratīkāra evāyam arthaḥ | yataḥ —

    paramam aviduṣāṃ padaṃ narāṇāṃpuravijayī karuṇāvidheyacetāḥkathayati bhagavān ihāntakāle,bhavabhayakātaratārakaṃ prabodham ||
    dambhaḥ

    satyam etat, tathāpi nāitat kāmakrodhābhibhūtānāṃ sambhāvyate! tathā hy udāharanti tairthikāḥ —

  • «yasya hastau ca pādau ca manaś cāiva susaṃyatam,vidyā tapaś ca kīrtiś ca sa tīrthaphalam aśnute |» iti ||

    • dambhaḥ — satyam etat, tathāpi nāitat kāmakrodhābhibhūtānāṃ sambhāvyate! tathā hy udāharanti tairthikāḥ —

    «yasya hastau ca pādau ca manaś cāiva susaṃyatam,vidyā tapaś ca kīrtiś ca sa tīrthaphalam aśnute |» iti ||
    ((nepathye))

    bho bhoḥ! paurāḥ! eṣa khalu saṃprāpto devo mahāmohaḥ! tena —

  • niṣyandaiś candanānāṃ sphaṭikamaṇiśilāvedikāḥ saṃskriyantāṃ,mucyantāṃ yantramārgāḥ pracaratu parito vāridhārā gṛheṣu!ucchrīyantāṃ samantāt sphuradurumaṇayaḥ śreṇayas toraṇānāṃ,dhūyantāṃ saudhamūrdhasv amarapatidhanurdhāmacitrāḥ patākāḥ ||

    • ((nepathye)) — bho bhoḥ! paurāḥ! eṣa khalu saṃprāpto devo mahāmohaḥ! tena —

    niṣyandaiś candanānāṃ sphaṭikamaṇiśilāvedikāḥ saṃskriyantāṃ,mucyantāṃ yantramārgāḥ pracaratu parito vāridhārā gṛheṣu!ucchrīyantāṃ samantāt sphuradurumaṇayaḥ śreṇayas toraṇānāṃ,dhūyantāṃ saudhamūrdhasv amarapatidhanurdhāmacitrāḥ patākāḥ ||
    dambhaḥ

    ārya! pratyāsanno 'yaṃ mahārājaḥ! tat pratyudgamanena saṃbhāvyatām āryeṇa |

    dambhaḥ — ārya! pratyāsanno 'yaṃ mahārājaḥ! tat pratyudgamanena saṃbhāvyatām āryeṇa |

    ahaṅkāraḥ

    evaṃ bhavatu | niṣkrāntau |

    viṣkambhakaḥ | tataḥ praviśati mahāmoho vibhavataś ca parivāraḥ |

    ahaṅkāraḥ — evaṃ bhavatu | ((niṣkrāntau |))

    ((viṣkambhakaḥ |))((tataḥ praviśati mahāmoho vibhavataś ca parivāraḥ |))

    mahāmohaḥ

    vihasya aho! niraṅkuśā jaḍadhiyaḥ!

  • ātmāsti dehād vyatiriktamūrtir bhoktā sa lokāntaritaḥ phalānām | —āśeyam ākāśataroḥ prasūnāt prathīyasaḥ svāduphalaprasūtau ||

    • idaṃ ca svakalpanāvinirmitapadārthāvaṣṭambhena jagad eva durvidagdhair vañcyate | tathā hi —

  • yan nāsty eva tad asti vastv iti mṛṣā jalpadbhir evāstikairvācālair bahubhis tu satyavacaso nindyāḥ kṛtā nāstikāḥ | haṃ ho! paśyata! tattvato yadi punaś chinnād ito varṣmaṇodṛṣṭaḥ kiṃ pariṇāmarūṣitaciter jīvaḥ pṛthak kair api?

    • api ca, na kevalaṃ jagad, ātmāiva tāvad amībhir vañcyate! tathā hi —

  • tulyatve vapuṣāṃ mukhādyavayavair varṇakramaḥ kīdṛśo?yoṣeyaṃ vasu vā parasya tad amuṃ bhedaṃ na vidmo vayam | hiṃsāyām athavā yatheṣṭagamane, strīṇāṃ parasvagrahe,kāryākāryakathāṃ tathāpi yad amī niṣpauruṣāḥ kurvate ||

    • vicintya, saślāgham | sarvathā lokāyatam eva śāstraṃ yatra pratyakśam eva pramāṇaṃ; pṛthivyaptejovāyavas tattvāni; arthakāmau puruṣārthau; bhūtany eva cetayante | nāsti paralokaḥ, mṛtyur evāpavargaḥ | tad etad asmadabhiprāyānubandhinā vācaspatinā praṇīya cārvākāya samarpitam | tena ca śiṣyopaśiṣyadvāreṇāsmiṃl loke bahulīkṛtaṃ tantram | tataḥ praviśati cārvākaḥ śiṣyaś ca

    mahāmohaḥ — ((vihasya)) aho! niraṅkuśā jaḍadhiyaḥ!

    ātmāsti dehād vyatiriktamūrtir bhoktā sa lokāntaritaḥ phalānām | —āśeyam ākāśataroḥ prasūnāt prathīyasaḥ svāduphalaprasūtau ||

    idaṃ ca svakalpanāvinirmitapadārthāvaṣṭambhena jagad eva durvidagdhair vañcyate | tathā hi —

    yan nāsty eva tad asti vastv iti mṛṣā jalpadbhir evāstikairvācālair bahubhis tu satyavacaso nindyāḥ kṛtā nāstikāḥ | haṃ ho! paśyata! tattvato yadi punaś chinnād ito varṣmaṇodṛṣṭaḥ kiṃ pariṇāmarūṣitaciter jīvaḥ pṛthak kair api?

    api ca, na kevalaṃ jagad, ātmāiva tāvad amībhir vañcyate! tathā hi —

    tulyatve vapuṣāṃ mukhādyavayavair varṇakramaḥ kīdṛśo?yoṣeyaṃ vasu vā parasya tad amuṃ bhedaṃ na vidmo vayam | hiṃsāyām athavā yatheṣṭagamane, strīṇāṃ parasvagrahe,kāryākāryakathāṃ tathāpi yad amī niṣpauruṣāḥ kurvate ||

    ((vicintya, saślāgham |)) sarvathā lokāyatam eva śāstraṃ yatra pratyakśam eva pramāṇaṃ; pṛthivyaptejovāyavas tattvāni; arthakāmau puruṣārthau; bhūtany eva cetayante | nāsti paralokaḥ, mṛtyur evāpavargaḥ | tad etad asmadabhiprāyānubandhinā vācaspatinā praṇīya cārvākāya samarpitam | tena ca śiṣyopaśiṣyadvāreṇāsmiṃl loke bahulīkṛtaṃ tantram | ((tataḥ praviśati cārvākaḥ śiṣyaś ca))

    cārvākaḥ

    vatsa, jānāsi daṇḍanītir eva vidyā! atrāiva vārtāntarbhavati | dhūrtapralāpas trayī! svargotpādakatvena viśeṣābhāvāt | paśya —

  • svargaḥ kartṛkriyādravyavināśe yadi yajvanām,tato dāvāgnidagdhānāṃ phalaṃ syad bhūri bhūruhām ||
  • api ca —
  • nihatasya paśor yajñe svargaprāptir yadīṣyate,svapitā yajamānena tatra kasmān na hanyate?
  • api ca —
  • mṛtānām api jantūnāṃ śrāddhaṃ cet tṛptikāraṇam,nirvāṇasya pradīpasya snehaḥ saṃvardhayec chikhāṃ?

    • cārvākaḥ — vatsa, jānāsi daṇḍanītir eva vidyā! atrāiva vārtāntarbhavati | dhūrtapralāpas trayī! svargotpādakatvena viśeṣābhāvāt | paśya —

    svargaḥ kartṛkriyādravyavināśe yadi yajvanām,tato dāvāgnidagdhānāṃ phalaṃ syad bhūri bhūruhām ||

    api ca —

    nihatasya paśor yajñe svargaprāptir yadīṣyate,svapitā yajamānena tatra kasmān na hanyate?

    api ca —

    mṛtānām api jantūnāṃ śrāddhaṃ cet tṛptikāraṇam,nirvāṇasya pradīpasya snehaḥ saṃvardhayec chikhāṃ?
    śiṣyaḥ

    ācālia, jaī eso evva puluattho jaṃ khajjae pijjaae, tā kitti edehiṃ titthiehiṃ saṃsālasokkhaṃ palihalia appā gholagholehiṃ palāasāṃtavaṇasaṭṭhakālāsaṇappahudihiṃ dukkhehiṃ khavijjadiācārya, yady eṣa eva puruṣārtho yat khādyate pīyate ca, tat kimity etais tairthikaiḥ saṃsārasaukhyaṃ parihṛtyātmā ghoraghoraiḥ parākasāntapanaṣaṣṭhakālāśanaprabhṛtibhir duḥkhaiḥ kṣapyate |

    śiṣyaḥ — ācālia, jaī eso evva puluattho jaṃ khajjae pijjaae, tā kitti edehiṃ titthiehiṃ saṃsālasokkhaṃ palihalia appā gholagholehiṃ palāasāṃtavaṇasaṭṭhakālāsaṇappahudihiṃ dukkhehiṃ khavijjadi (ācārya, yady eṣa eva puruṣārtho yat khādyate pīyate ca, tat kimity etais tairthikaiḥ saṃsārasaukhyaṃ parihṛtyātmā ghoraghoraiḥ parākasāntapanaṣaṣṭhakālāśanaprabhṛtibhir duḥkhaiḥ kṣapyate |)

    cārvākaḥ

    dhūrtapraṇītāgamapratāritānām mūrkhāṇām āśāmodakair eveyaṃ tṛptir! paśya paśya —

  • kvāliṅganaṃ bhujanipīḍitabāhumūlabhagnonnatastanamanoharam āyatākṣyāḥ,bhikṣopavāsaniyamārkamarīcidāhairdehopaśoṣaṇavidhiḥ kudhiyāṃ kva cāiṣaḥ?

    • cārvākaḥ — dhūrtapraṇītāgamapratāritānām mūrkhāṇām āśāmodakair eveyaṃ tṛptir! paśya paśya —

    kvāliṅganaṃ bhujanipīḍitabāhumūlabhagnonnatastanamanoharam āyatākṣyāḥ,bhikṣopavāsaniyamārkamarīcidāhairdehopaśoṣaṇavidhiḥ kudhiyāṃ kva cāiṣaḥ?
    śiṣyaḥ

    ācālia, evaṃ khu titthia ālavanti dukkhamissidaṃ saṃsālasokkhaṃ palihalaṇijjaṃ tti |ācārya, evaṃ khalu tairthikā ālapanti duḥkhamiśritaṃ saṃsārasaukhyaṃ pariharaṇīyam iti |

    śiṣyaḥ — ācālia, evaṃ khu titthia ālavanti dukkhamissidaṃ saṃsālasokkhaṃ palihalaṇijjaṃ tti | (ācārya, evaṃ khalu tairthikā ālapanti duḥkhamiśritaṃ saṃsārasaukhyaṃ pariharaṇīyam iti |)

    cārvākaḥ

    vihasya āḥ! durbuddhivilasitam idaṃ narapaśūnām!

  • «tyājyaṃ sukhaṃ viṣayasaṃgamajanma puṃsāṃduḥkhopasṛṣṭam» — iti mūrkhavicāraṇāiṣā | vrīhīn jihāsati sitottamataṇḍulāḍhyānko nāma bhos tuṣakaṇopahitān hitārthī?

    • cārvākaḥ — ((vihasya)) āḥ! durbuddhivilasitam idaṃ narapaśūnām!

    «tyājyaṃ sukhaṃ viṣayasaṃgamajanma puṃsāṃduḥkhopasṛṣṭam» — iti mūrkhavicāraṇāiṣā | vrīhīn jihāsati sitottamataṇḍulāḍhyānko nāma bhos tuṣakaṇopahitān hitārthī?
    mahāmohaḥ

    aye, cireṇa khalu pramāṇavanti vacanāni karṇasukham upajanayanti! vilokya sānandam | hanta! priyasuhṛn me, cārvākaḥ!

    mahāmohaḥ — aye, cireṇa khalu pramāṇavanti vacanāni karṇasukham upajanayanti! ((vilokya sānandam |)) hanta! priyasuhṛn me, cārvākaḥ!

    cārvākaḥ

    vilokya eṣa mahārājamahāmohaḥ! upasarpāmi | upasṛtya jayatu jayatu mahārājaḥ! eṣa cārvākaḥ praṇamati |

    cārvākaḥ — ((vilokya)) eṣa mahārājamahāmohaḥ! upasarpāmi | ((upasṛtya)) jayatu jayatu mahārājaḥ! eṣa cārvākaḥ praṇamati |

    mahāmohaḥ

    cārvāka, svāgataṃ te! ihopaviśyatām |

    mahāmohaḥ — cārvāka, svāgataṃ te! ihopaviśyatām |

    cārvākaḥ

    upaviśya deva! kaler asāv aṣṭāṅgapātaḥ praṇāmaḥ |

    cārvākaḥ — ((upaviśya)) deva! kaler asāv aṣṭāṅgapātaḥ praṇāmaḥ |

    mahāmohaḥ

    atha kaler bhadram avyāhatam |

    mahāmohaḥ — atha kaler bhadram avyāhatam |

    cārvākaḥ

    devaprasādena kaler bhadram! nirvartitakartavyaśeṣaś ca devapādamūlaṃ draṣṭum icchati | yataḥ —

  • ājñām avāpya mahatīṃ dviṣatāṃ nikhātānnirvartya tāṃ sapadi labdhasukhaprasādaḥ | uccaiḥ pramodam anumoditadarśanaḥ sandhanyo namasyati padāmburuhaṃ prabhūṇām ||

    • cārvākaḥ — devaprasādena kaler bhadram! nirvartitakartavyaśeṣaś ca devapādamūlaṃ draṣṭum icchati | yataḥ —

    ājñām avāpya mahatīṃ dviṣatāṃ nikhātānnirvartya tāṃ sapadi labdhasukhaprasādaḥ | uccaiḥ pramodam anumoditadarśanaḥ sandhanyo namasyati padāmburuhaṃ prabhūṇām ||
    mahāmohaḥ

    atha tatra kiyat saṃpannam?

    mahāmohaḥ — atha tatra kiyat saṃpannam?

    cārvākaḥ

    deva —

  • vyatītavedārthapathaḥ prathīyasīṃ,yatheṣṭhaceṣṭhāṃ gamito mahājanaḥ | tad atra hetur na kalir na cāpy ahaṃ,prabhuprasādo hi tanoti pauruṣam ||

    • tatrottarāḥ pathikāḥ pāścātyāś ca trayīm eva tyājitāḥ | śamadamādīnāṃ kāiva kathā? anyatrāpi prāyaśo jīvikāmātraphalāiva trayī | yathāhācāryaḥ —

  • agnihotraṃ trayo vedās tridaṇḍaṃ bhasmaguṇṭhanam —buddhipauruṣahīnānāṃ jīviketi bṛhaspatiḥ ||

    • tena kurukṣetrādiṣu tīrtheṣu tāvad devena svapne'pi vidyāprabodhodayo nāśaṅkanīyaḥ |

    cārvākaḥ — deva —

    vyatītavedārthapathaḥ prathīyasīṃ,yatheṣṭhaceṣṭhāṃ gamito mahājanaḥ | tad atra hetur na kalir na cāpy ahaṃ,prabhuprasādo hi tanoti pauruṣam ||

    tatrottarāḥ pathikāḥ pāścātyāś ca trayīm eva tyājitāḥ | śamadamādīnāṃ kāiva kathā? anyatrāpi prāyaśo jīvikāmātraphalāiva trayī | yathāhācāryaḥ —

    agnihotraṃ trayo vedās tridaṇḍaṃ bhasmaguṇṭhanam —buddhipauruṣahīnānāṃ jīviketi bṛhaspatiḥ ||

    tena kurukṣetrādiṣu tīrtheṣu tāvad devena svapne'pi vidyāprabodhodayo nāśaṅkanīyaḥ |

    mahāmohaḥ

    sādhu! saṃpāditam! mahat khalu tat tīrthaṃ vyarthīkṛtam |

    mahāmohaḥ — sādhu! saṃpāditam! mahat khalu tat tīrthaṃ vyarthīkṛtam |

    cārvākaḥ

    deva, anyac ca vijñāpyam asti |

    cārvākaḥ — deva, anyac ca vijñāpyam asti |

    mahāmohaḥ

    kiṃ tat?

    mahāmohaḥ — kiṃ tat?

    cārvākaḥ

    asti viṣṇubhaktir nāma mahāprabhāvā yoginī | sā tu kalinā yady api viralapracārā kṛtā, tathāpi tadanugṛhītān vayam ālokayitum api na prabhavāmaḥ | tad atra devenāvadhātavyam iti |

    cārvākaḥ — asti viṣṇubhaktir nāma mahāprabhāvā yoginī | sā tu kalinā yady api viralapracārā kṛtā, tathāpi tadanugṛhītān vayam ālokayitum api na prabhavāmaḥ | tad atra devenāvadhātavyam iti |

    mahāmohaḥ

    sabhayam ātmagatam | āḥ! prasiddhamahāprabhāvā sā yoginī, svabhāvād vidveṣiṇī cāsmākaṃ | durucchedā sā | prakāśam | bhadra, alam anayā śaṅkayā | kāmakrodhādiṣu pratipakṣeṣu kutreyam udeṣyati? tathāpi laghīyasy api ripau nānavahitena jigīṣuṇā bhavitavyam | yataḥ —

  • vipākadāruṇo rājñāṃ ripur alpo 'py aruṃtudaḥ,udvejayati sūkṣmo 'pi caraṇaṃ kaṇṭakāṅkuraḥ ||

    • nepathyābhumukham avalokya ko 'tra bhoḥ? praviśya dauvārikaḥ |

    mahāmohaḥ — ((sabhayam ātmagatam |)) āḥ! prasiddhamahāprabhāvā sā yoginī, svabhāvād vidveṣiṇī cāsmākaṃ | durucchedā sā | ((prakāśam |)) bhadra, alam anayā śaṅkayā | kāmakrodhādiṣu pratipakṣeṣu kutreyam udeṣyati? tathāpi laghīyasy api ripau nānavahitena jigīṣuṇā bhavitavyam | yataḥ —

    vipākadāruṇo rājñāṃ ripur alpo 'py aruṃtudaḥ,udvejayati sūkṣmo 'pi caraṇaṃ kaṇṭakāṅkuraḥ ||

    ((nepathyābhumukham avalokya)) ko 'tra bhoḥ? ((praviśya dauvārikaḥ |))

    dauvārikaḥ

    jayatu, jayatu! ājñāpayatu devaḥ!

    dauvārikaḥ — jayatu, jayatu! ājñāpayatu devaḥ!

    mahāmohaḥ

    bho! asatsaṅga! ādiśyatāṃ kāmakrodhalobhamadamātsaryādayo yathā — yoginī viṣṇubhaktir bhavadbhir evāvahitair vihantavyeti |

    mahāmohaḥ — bho! asatsaṅga! ādiśyatāṃ kāmakrodhalobhamadamātsaryādayo yathā — yoginī viṣṇubhaktir bhavadbhir evāvahitair vihantavyeti |

    dauvārikaḥ

    yad ājñāpayati devaḥ | iti niṣkrāntaḥ | tataḥ praviśati patrahastaḥ puruṣaḥ

    dauvārikaḥ — yad ājñāpayati devaḥ | ((iti niṣkrāntaḥ |)) ((tataḥ praviśati patrahastaḥ puruṣaḥ))

    puruṣaḥ

    ˹ahake ukkaladesādo āado mhi | tattha sāalatīlasaṇṇivese pulisottamasaggidaṃ devadāadaṇam | tassiṃ madamāṇehiṃ bhaṭṭakehiṃ mahālāasaāsaṃ pesido mhi | vilokya esā vālāṇasī | edaṃ lāaulam | jāva ppavisāmi | praviśya eso bhaṭṭako, cavvākeṇa satthaṃ kiṃvi mantaanto ciṭṭhadi | bhodu uvasappāmi ṇam | upsṛtya jedu, jedu, bhaṭṭako! edaṃ pattaṃ ṇilūpañjadu bhaṭṭako |˼ iti patram arpayati(aham utkaladeśād āgato 'smi | tatra sāgaratīrasanniveśe puruṣottamaśabditaṃ devatāyatanam | tasmin madamānābhyāṃ bhaṭṭārakābhyāṃ mahārājasakāśaṃ preṣito 'smi | eṣā vārāṇasī | etad rājakulam | yāvat praviśāmi | eṣa bhaṭṭārakaś cārvākeṇa sārdhaṃ kimapi mantrayaṃs tiṣṭhati | bhavatūpasarpāmy enam | jayatu jayatu bhaṭṭāṛakaḥ | idaṃ patraṃ nirūpayata bhaṭṭārakaḥ |)

    puruṣaḥ — ˹ahake ukkaladesādo āado mhi | tattha sāalatīlasaṇṇivese pulisottamasaggidaṃ devadāadaṇam | tassiṃ madamāṇehiṃ bhaṭṭakehiṃ mahālāasaāsaṃ pesido mhi | ((vilokya)) esā vālāṇasī | edaṃ lāaulam | jāva ppavisāmi | ((praviśya)) eso bhaṭṭako, cavvākeṇa satthaṃ kiṃvi mantaanto ciṭṭhadi | bhodu uvasappāmi ṇam | ((upsṛtya)) jedu, jedu, bhaṭṭako! edaṃ pattaṃ ṇilūpañjadu bhaṭṭako |˼ ((iti patram arpayati))(aham utkaladeśād āgato 'smi | tatra sāgaratīrasanniveśe puruṣottamaśabditaṃ devatāyatanam | tasmin madamānābhyāṃ bhaṭṭārakābhyāṃ mahārājasakāśaṃ preṣito 'smi | eṣā vārāṇasī | etad rājakulam | yāvat praviśāmi | eṣa bhaṭṭārakaś cārvākeṇa sārdhaṃ kimapi mantrayaṃs tiṣṭhati | bhavatūpasarpāmy enam | jayatu jayatu bhaṭṭāṛakaḥ | idaṃ patraṃ nirūpayata bhaṭṭārakaḥ |)

    mahāmohaḥ

    patraṃ gṛhītvā kuto bhavān?

    mahāmohaḥ — ((patraṃ gṛhītvā)) kuto bhavān?

    puruṣaḥ

    bhaṭṭaka! pulisottamādo |bhaṭṭāraka! puruṣottamād |

    puruṣaḥ — bhaṭṭaka! pulisottamādo | (bhaṭṭāraka! puruṣottamād |)

    mahāmohaḥ

    svāgatam kāryam atyāhitaṃ bhaviṣyati | prakāśam cārvāka! gaccha! kartavyeṣv avahitena bhavatā bhavitavyam |

    mahāmohaḥ — ((svāgatam)) kāryam atyāhitaṃ bhaviṣyati | ((prakāśam)) cārvāka! gaccha! kartavyeṣv avahitena bhavatā bhavitavyam |

    cārvākaḥ

    yad ājñāpayati devaḥ | iti niṣkrāntaḥ

    cārvākaḥ — yad ājñāpayati devaḥ | ((iti niṣkrāntaḥ))

    mahāmohaḥ

    patraṃ vācayatisvasti! śrīvārāṇasyāṃ mahārājādhirājaparameśvaramahāmohapādān puruṣottamāyatanād madamānau sāṣṭāṅgapātaṃ praṇamya vijñāpayataḥ | yathā bhadram avyāhatam! anyac ca, devī śāntir mātrā śraddhayā saha, vivekasya dautyam āpannā, vivekasaṃgamāya devīm upaniṣadam ahar niśaṃ pratibodhayati | api ca kāmasahacaro 'pi, dharmo vairāgyādibhir upajapta iva lakṣyate | yataḥ, kāmād vibhidya kutaścin nigūḍhaḥ pracarati | tad etaj jñātvā, tatra devaḥ pramāṇam iti |

    mahāmohaḥ — ((patraṃ vācayati))svasti! śrīvārāṇasyāṃ mahārājādhirājaparameśvaramahāmohapādān puruṣottamāyatanād madamānau sāṣṭāṅgapātaṃ praṇamya vijñāpayataḥ | yathā bhadram avyāhatam! anyac ca, devī śāntir mātrā śraddhayā saha, vivekasya dautyam āpannā, vivekasaṃgamāya devīm upaniṣadam ahar niśaṃ pratibodhayati | api ca kāmasahacaro 'pi, dharmo vairāgyādibhir upajapta iva lakṣyate | yataḥ, kāmād vibhidya kutaścin nigūḍhaḥ pracarati | tad etaj jñātvā, tatra devaḥ pramāṇam iti |

    mahāmohaḥ

    sakrodham āḥ! kim evam atimugdhau śānter api bibhītaḥ? kāmādiṣu pratipakṣeṣu kuto 'syāḥ saṃbhavaḥ? tathā hi —

  • dhātā viśvavisṛṣṭimātranirato; devo 'pi gaurībhujaśleṣānandavighūrṇamānanayano dakṣādhvaradhvaṃsanaḥ;daityāriḥ kamalākapolamakarīlekhāṅkitoraḥsthalaḥśete 'bdhāv | itareṣu janteṣu punaḥ kā nāma śānteḥ kathā?

    • puruṣaṃ prati vadati jālma, gaccha! kāmaṃ satvaram upetyādeśam asmākaṃ pratipādaya yathā — durāśayo dharma ity asmābhir avagatam | tad asmin muhūrtam api na viśvasitavyam | dṛḍhaṃ baddhvā dhārayitavya iti |

    mahāmohaḥ — ((sakrodham)) āḥ! kim evam atimugdhau śānter api bibhītaḥ? kāmādiṣu pratipakṣeṣu kuto 'syāḥ saṃbhavaḥ? tathā hi —

    dhātā viśvavisṛṣṭimātranirato; devo 'pi gaurībhujaśleṣānandavighūrṇamānanayano dakṣādhvaradhvaṃsanaḥ;daityāriḥ kamalākapolamakarīlekhāṅkitoraḥsthalaḥśete 'bdhāv | itareṣu janteṣu punaḥ kā nāma śānteḥ kathā?

    ((puruṣaṃ prati vadati)) jālma, gaccha! kāmaṃ satvaram upetyādeśam asmākaṃ pratipādaya yathā — durāśayo dharma ity asmābhir avagatam | tad asmin muhūrtam api na viśvasitavyam | dṛḍhaṃ baddhvā dhārayitavya iti |

    puruṣaḥ

    ˹jaṃ devo āṇavedi |˼ iti niṣkrāntaḥ(yad deva ājñāpayati |)

    puruṣaḥ — ˹jaṃ devo āṇavedi |˼ ((iti niṣkrāntaḥ))(yad deva ājñāpayati |)

    mahāmohaḥ

    svagataṃ vicintya śānteḥ ko 'bhyupāyaḥ? athavā alam upāyāntareṇa! krodhalobhāv eva tāvad atra paryāptau | prakāśam kaḥ ko 'tra bhoḥ? praviśya dauvārikaḥ

    mahāmohaḥ — ((svagataṃ vicintya)) śānteḥ ko 'bhyupāyaḥ? athavā alam upāyāntareṇa! krodhalobhāv eva tāvad atra paryāptau | ((prakāśam)) kaḥ ko 'tra bhoḥ? ((praviśya dauvārikaḥ))

    dauvārikaḥ

    ājñāpayatu devaḥ |

    dauvārikaḥ — ājñāpayatu devaḥ |

    mahāmohaḥ

    tāvad āhūyatāṃ krodho lobhāś ca |

    mahāmohaḥ — tāvad āhūyatāṃ krodho lobhāś ca |

    dauvārikaḥ

    yad ājñāpayati devaḥ | iti niṣkrāntaḥ tataḥ praviśati krodho lobhaś ca

    dauvārikaḥ — yad ājñāpayati devaḥ | ((iti niṣkrāntaḥ)) ((tataḥ praviśati krodho lobhaś ca))

    krodhaḥ

    śrutaṃ mayā śāntiśraddhāviṣṇubhaktayo mahārājasya pratipakṣam ācarantīti | aho! mayi jīvati katham āsām ātmanirapekṣitaṃ ceṣṭitam? tathā hi —

  • andhīkaromi bhuvanaṃ, badhirīkaromi | dhīraṃ sacetanam, acetanatāṃ nayāmi | kṛtyaṃ na paśyati, na yena hitaṃ śṛṇoti,dhīmān adhītam api na pratisaṃdadhāti ||

    • krodhaḥ — śrutaṃ mayā śāntiśraddhāviṣṇubhaktayo mahārājasya pratipakṣam ācarantīti | aho! mayi jīvati katham āsām ātmanirapekṣitaṃ ceṣṭitam? tathā hi —

    andhīkaromi bhuvanaṃ, badhirīkaromi | dhīraṃ sacetanam, acetanatāṃ nayāmi | kṛtyaṃ na paśyati, na yena hitaṃ śṛṇoti,dhīmān adhītam api na pratisaṃdadhāti ||
    lobhaḥ

    are! madupagṛhītā manorathasaritparamparām api tāvan na tariṣyanti kiṃ punaḥ śāntyādīṃś cintayiṣyanti? paśya —

  • santy ete mama dantino madajalapramlānagaṇḍasthalā | vātavyāyatapātinaś ca turagā — bhūyo 'pi lapsye 'parān!etal labdham, idaṃ labhe; punar idaṃ labdhvādhikaṃ dhyāyatāṃcintājarjaracetasāṃ bata nṛṇāṃ, kā nāma śānteḥ kathā?

    • lobhaḥ — are! madupagṛhītā manorathasaritparamparām api tāvan na tariṣyanti kiṃ punaḥ śāntyādīṃś cintayiṣyanti? paśya —

    santy ete mama dantino madajalapramlānagaṇḍasthalā | vātavyāyatapātinaś ca turagā — bhūyo 'pi lapsye 'parān!etal labdham, idaṃ labhe; punar idaṃ labdhvādhikaṃ dhyāyatāṃcintājarjaracetasāṃ bata nṛṇāṃ, kā nāma śānteḥ kathā?
    krodhaḥ

    sakhe, viditas tvayā matprabhāvaḥ —

  • tvāṣṭraṃ vṛtram aghātayat surapatiś, candrārdhacūḍo 'cchinaddevo brahmaśiro, vasiṣṭhatanayān āghātayat kauśikaḥ ||
  • api cāhaṃ —
  • vidyāvanty api, kīrtimanty api, sadācārāvadātāny api,proccaiḥ pauruṣabhūṣaṇāny api, kulāny uddhartum īśaḥ kṣaṇāt ||

    • krodhaḥ — sakhe, viditas tvayā matprabhāvaḥ —

    tvāṣṭraṃ vṛtram aghātayat surapatiś, candrārdhacūḍo 'cchinaddevo brahmaśiro, vasiṣṭhatanayān āghātayat kauśikaḥ ||

    api cāhaṃ —

    vidyāvanty api, kīrtimanty api, sadācārāvadātāny api,proccaiḥ pauruṣabhūṣaṇāny api, kulāny uddhartum īśaḥ kṣaṇāt ||
    lobhaḥ

    tṛṣṇe, itas tāvat! praviśya tṛṣṇā |

    lobhaḥ — tṛṣṇe, itas tāvat! ((praviśya tṛṣṇā |))

    tṛṣṇā

    kiṃ ajjaütto āṇavedu?āryaputra ājñāpayatu |

    tṛṣṇā — kiṃ ajjaütto āṇavedu? (āryaputra ājñāpayatu |)

    lobhaḥ

    priye, śrūyatām —

  • kṣetragrāmavanādripattanapuradvīpakṣamāṇḍalapratyāśāyatasūtrabaddhamanasāṃ labdhādhikaṃ dhyāyatāṃ,tṛṣṇe devi, yadi prasīdasi, tanoṣy aṅgāni tuṅgāni cet,tad bhoḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ kutaḥ śamakathā brahmāṇḍalakṣair api?

    • lobhaḥ — priye, śrūyatām —

    kṣetragrāmavanādripattanapuradvīpakṣamāṇḍalapratyāśāyatasūtrabaddhamanasāṃ labdhādhikaṃ dhyāyatāṃ,tṛṣṇe devi, yadi prasīdasi, tanoṣy aṅgāni tuṅgāni cet,tad bhoḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ kutaḥ śamakathā brahmāṇḍalakṣair api?
    tṛṣṇā

    ajjaütta, saaṃ jevva dāva ahaṃ edassiṃ atthe ṇiccaṃ ahijutta | saṃpadaṃ ajjaüttassa aṇṇāe bahmaṇḍakoḍīhiṃ pi ṇa me udaraṃ pūraïssaṃdi!āryaputra, svayam eva tāvad aham etasminn arthe nityam abhiyuktā | sāṃpratam āryaputrasyājñayā brahmaṇḍakoṭibhir api na me udaraṃ pūrayiṣyate |

    tṛṣṇā — ajjaütta, saaṃ jevva dāva ahaṃ edassiṃ atthe ṇiccaṃ ahijutta | saṃpadaṃ ajjaüttassa aṇṇāe bahmaṇḍakoḍīhiṃ pi ṇa me udaraṃ pūraïssaṃdi! (āryaputra, svayam eva tāvad aham etasminn arthe nityam abhiyuktā | sāṃpratam āryaputrasyājñayā brahmaṇḍakoṭibhir api na me udaraṃ pūrayiṣyate |)

    krodhaḥ

    hiṃse, itas tāvat! praviśya hiṃsā

    krodhaḥ — hiṃse, itas tāvat! ((praviśya hiṃsā))

    hiṃsā

    esa mhi! āṇavedu ajjaütto!eṣāsmi! ājñāpayatv āryaputraḥ!

    hiṃsā — esa mhi! āṇavedu ajjaütto! (eṣāsmi! ājñāpayatv āryaputraḥ!)

    krodhaḥ

    priye, sahadharmacāriṇyā tvayā, mātṛpitṛvadho 'pi mameṣatkara eva! tathā hi —

  • keyaṃ mātā? piśācī! ka iva hi janako? bhrātaraḥ ke 'tra? kīṭā!vandhyo 'yaṃ bandhuvargaḥ | kuṭilaviṭasuhṛcceṣṭitā jñātayo 'mī ||

    • hastau niṣpīḍya

  • āgarbhaṃ yāvad eṣāṃ kulam idam akhilaṃ nāiva niḥśeṣayāmi | sphurjantaḥ krodhavahner na dadhati viratiṃ tāvad aṅge sphuliṅgāḥ ||

    • vilokya eṣa svāmī! tad upasarpāmaḥ!

    krodhaḥ — priye, sahadharmacāriṇyā tvayā, mātṛpitṛvadho 'pi mameṣatkara eva! tathā hi —

    keyaṃ mātā? piśācī! ka iva hi janako? bhrātaraḥ ke 'tra? kīṭā!vandhyo 'yaṃ bandhuvargaḥ | kuṭilaviṭasuhṛcceṣṭitā jñātayo 'mī ||

    ((hastau niṣpīḍya))

    āgarbhaṃ yāvad eṣāṃ kulam idam akhilaṃ nāiva niḥśeṣayāmi | sphurjantaḥ krodhavahner na dadhati viratiṃ tāvad aṅge sphuliṅgāḥ ||

    ((vilokya)) eṣa svāmī! tad upasarpāmaḥ!

    sarve

    upasṛtya jayatu, jayatu, devaḥ!

    sarve — ((upasṛtya)) jayatu, jayatu, devaḥ!

    mahāmohaḥ

    śraddhāyās tanayā śāntir asmaddveṣiṇī | sā bhavadbhir avahitair nigrāhyā |

    mahāmohaḥ — śraddhāyās tanayā śāntir asmaddveṣiṇī | sā bhavadbhir avahitair nigrāhyā |

    sarve

    yad ādiśati devaḥ | iti niṣkrāntāḥ

    sarve — yad ādiśati devaḥ | ((iti niṣkrāntāḥ))

    mahāmohaḥ

    śraddhāyās tanayā — ity upakṣepeṇopāyāntaram api hṛdayam ārūḍham | tathā hi, śānter mātā śraddhā, sā ca paratantrā | tat kenāpy upāyenopaniṣatsakāśāt tāvac chraddhāpakarṣaṇaṃ kartavyam | tato mātṛviyogaduḥkhād atimṛdulatarā śāntir uparatā bhaviṣyati, avasīdantī vā viraṃsyati | śraddhāṃ cākraṣṭuṃ mithyādṛṣṭir eva vilāsinī pragalbheti tasmin viṣaye sāiva niyojyā | pārśvato vilokya | vibhramāvati! satvaram āhūyatāṃ mithyādṛṣṭivilāsinī!

    mahāmohaḥ — śraddhāyās tanayā — ity upakṣepeṇopāyāntaram api hṛdayam ārūḍham | tathā hi, śānter mātā śraddhā, sā ca paratantrā | tat kenāpy upāyenopaniṣatsakāśāt tāvac chraddhāpakarṣaṇaṃ kartavyam | tato mātṛviyogaduḥkhād atimṛdulatarā śāntir uparatā bhaviṣyati, avasīdantī vā viraṃsyati | śraddhāṃ cākraṣṭuṃ mithyādṛṣṭir eva vilāsinī pragalbheti tasmin viṣaye sāiva niyojyā | ((pārśvato vilokya |)) vibhramāvati! satvaram āhūyatāṃ mithyādṛṣṭivilāsinī!

    vibhramāvatī

    jaṃ devo āṇavedi |yad deva ājñāpayati | niṣkramya mithyādṛṣṭyā saha praviśati

    vibhramāvatī — jaṃ devo āṇavedi | (yad deva ājñāpayati |)((niṣkramya mithyādṛṣṭyā saha praviśati))

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    sahi, ciradiṭṭhassa mahārāassa kahaṃ muhaṃ pekkhissaṃ? ṇaṃ mahārāo maṃ uvālambhissadi |sakhi, ciradṛṣṭasya mahārājasya kathaṃ mukhaṃ prekṣiṣye? nanu mahārājo māṃ upālambhiṣyate |

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — sahi, ciradiṭṭhassa mahārāassa kahaṃ muhaṃ pekkhissaṃ? ṇaṃ mahārāo maṃ uvālambhissadi | (sakhi, ciradṛṣṭasya mahārājasya kathaṃ mukhaṃ prekṣiṣye? nanu mahārājo māṃ upālambhiṣyate |)

    vibhramāvatī

    sahi, tuha daṃsaṇe appāṇaṃ pi mahārāo ṇa cedaïssadi, tado kahaṃ uvālambhissadi?sakhi, tvaddarśane ātmānam api mahārājo na cetayiṣyati, tataḥ kathaṃ upālambhiṣyate?

    vibhramāvatī — sahi, tuha daṃsaṇe appāṇaṃ pi mahārāo ṇa cedaïssadi, tado kahaṃ uvālambhissadi? (sakhi, tvaddarśane ātmānam api mahārājo na cetayiṣyati, tataḥ kathaṃ upālambhiṣyate?)

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    kīsa maṃ alīasohaggāṃ saṃbhāvia viḍambesi?kasmān mām alīkasaubhāgyāṃ saṃbhāvya viḍambayasi?

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — kīsa maṃ alīasohaggāṃ saṃbhāvia viḍambesi? (kasmān mām alīkasaubhāgyāṃ saṃbhāvya viḍambayasi?)

    vibhramāvatī

    sahi, saṃpadaṃ jevva pekkhissaṃ aliattaṇaṃ sohaggassa | aṇṇaṃ ca ghuṇṇantaṇiddāulaṃ via ppiasahīe loaṇaṃ pekkhāmi | tā kiṃ khu ppiasahīe viṇiddadāe kālaṇam?sakhi, sāṃpratam eva prekṣiṣye 'līkatvaṃ saubhāgyasya | anyac ca ghūrṇamānanidrākulaṃ iva priyasakhyā locanaṃ prekṣye | tat kiṃ khalu priyasakhyā vinidratāyāḥ kāraṇam?

    vibhramāvatī — sahi, saṃpadaṃ jevva pekkhissaṃ aliattaṇaṃ sohaggassa | aṇṇaṃ ca ghuṇṇantaṇiddāulaṃ via ppiasahīe loaṇaṃ pekkhāmi | tā kiṃ khu ppiasahīe viṇiddadāe kālaṇam? (sakhi, sāṃpratam eva prekṣiṣye 'līkatvaṃ saubhāgyasya | anyac ca ghūrṇamānanidrākulaṃ iva priyasakhyā locanaṃ prekṣye | tat kiṃ khalu priyasakhyā vinidratāyāḥ kāraṇam?)

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    ekavallahā vi jā itthiā hoi tāe vi ṇiddā dullahā ṇāma | kiṃ uṇa amhāṇaṃ saalavallahāṇam?sakhi, ekavallabhāpi yā strī bhavati tasyā api nidrā durlabhā nāma | kiṃ punar asmākaṃ sakalavallabhānām?

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — ekavallahā vi jā itthiā hoi tāe vi ṇiddā dullahā ṇāma | kiṃ uṇa amhāṇaṃ saalavallahāṇam? (sakhi, ekavallabhāpi yā strī bhavati tasyā api nidrā durlabhā nāma | kiṃ punar asmākaṃ sakalavallabhānām?)

    vibhramāvatī

    ke uṇa piasahīe vallahā?ke punaḥ priyasakhyā vallabhāḥ?

    vibhramāvatī — ke uṇa piasahīe vallahā? (ke punaḥ priyasakhyā vallabhāḥ?)

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    mahārāo, tado uvari kāmo, koho, loho a | ahava alaṃ viseseṇa! ettha ule jo jādo hiaaṇihidae rattidiahāi ahiramaī mae ṇa viṇābālo ṭhaviro juvāṇo a |mahārājaḥ, tata upari kāmaḥ, krodho, lobhaś ca | athavālaṃ viśeṣeṇa! atra kule yo jāto hṛdayanihitayā rātridivasāy abhiramate mayā na vinā — bālaḥ sthavīro yuvānaś ca |

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — mahārāo, tado uvari kāmo, koho, loho a | ahava alaṃ viseseṇa! ettha ule jo jādo hiaaṇihidae rattidiahāi ahiramaī mae ṇa viṇābālo ṭhaviro juvāṇo a | (mahārājaḥ, tata upari kāmaḥ, krodho, lobhaś ca | athavālaṃ viśeṣeṇa! atra kule yo jāto hṛdayanihitayā rātridivasāy abhiramate mayā na vinā — bālaḥ sthavīro yuvānaś ca |)

    vibhramāvatī

    ṇaṃ kāmassa raï, kohassa hiṃsā, lohassa tiṇhā paramappia suṇiadi | tāsaṃ kadhaṃ piajaṇaṃ ṇiccaṃ ramaantī issaṃ ṇa jāṇesi?nanu kāmasya ratiḥ, krodhasya hiṃsā, lobhasya tṛṣṇā priyeti śrūyate | tāsāṃ kathaṃ priyajanān nityaṃ ramayantīrṣyāṃ na janayasi?

    vibhramāvatī — ṇaṃ kāmassa raï, kohassa hiṃsā, lohassa tiṇhā paramappia suṇiadi | tāsaṃ kadhaṃ piajaṇaṃ ṇiccaṃ ramaantī issaṃ ṇa jāṇesi? (nanu kāmasya ratiḥ, krodhasya hiṃsā, lobhasya tṛṣṇā priyeti śrūyate | tāsāṃ kathaṃ priyajanān nityaṃ ramayantīrṣyāṃ na janayasi?)

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    issatti kiṃ bhaṇiadi? tāo vi mae viṇā muhuttaṃ vi ṇa tussanti!īrṣyeti kiṃ bhaṇyate? tā api mayā vinā muhūrtam api na tuṣyanti!

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — issatti kiṃ bhaṇiadi? tāo vi mae viṇā muhuttaṃ vi ṇa tussanti! (īrṣyeti kiṃ bhaṇyate? tā api mayā vinā muhūrtam api na tuṣyanti!)

    vibhramāvatī

    ado jevva bhaṇāmi tuha sarisī suhaā iha puhivīe ṇatthi tti, jāe sohaggaveragg'uijariahiaāo savattīo vi sampasādaṃ paḍicchanti | sahi, aṇṇaṃ vi bhaṇāmi | evaṃ ṇiddāulahiaā visaṃṭhulakkhalantacalaṇaneurajhaṃkāramuharāe gadīe mahārāaṃ saṃbhāvaaṃtī saṃkidahiaaṃ karissadi piasahitti takkemi |ata eva bhaṇāmi tava sadṛśī subhagā iha pṛthivyāṃ nāstīti, yasyāḥ saubhāgyavairāgyavijvaritahṛdayāḥ sapatnyo 'pi saṃprasādaṃ pratīcchanti | sakhi, anyad api bhaṇāmi | evaṃ nidrākulahṛdayā visaṃsthulaskhalaccaraṇanūpurajhaṅkāramukharayā gatyā mahārājaṃ saṃbhāvayantī śaṅkitahṛdayaṃ kariṣyati priyasakhīti tarkayāmi |

    vibhramāvatī — ado jevva bhaṇāmi tuha sarisī suhaā iha puhivīe ṇatthi tti, jāe sohaggaveragg'uijariahiaāo savattīo vi sampasādaṃ paḍicchanti | sahi, aṇṇaṃ vi bhaṇāmi | evaṃ ṇiddāulahiaā visaṃṭhulakkhalantacalaṇaneurajhaṃkāramuharāe gadīe mahārāaṃ saṃbhāvaaṃtī saṃkidahiaaṃ karissadi piasahitti takkemi | (ata eva bhaṇāmi tava sadṛśī subhagā iha pṛthivyāṃ nāstīti, yasyāḥ saubhāgyavairāgyavijvaritahṛdayāḥ sapatnyo 'pi saṃprasādaṃ pratīcchanti | sakhi, anyad api bhaṇāmi | evaṃ nidrākulahṛdayā visaṃsthulaskhalaccaraṇanūpurajhaṅkāramukharayā gatyā mahārājaṃ saṃbhāvayantī śaṅkitahṛdayaṃ kariṣyati priyasakhīti tarkayāmi |)

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    kiṃ ettha saṃkidavvaṃ? ṇaṃ amhāṇaṃ mahārāaṇiuttāṇaṃ jevva eso aviṇao | avi a, daṃsaṇamattappasādiapurusāṇaṃ juvaīṇaṃ kerisaṃ bhaam?kim atra śaṅkitavyam? na cāsmākaṃ mahārājaniyuktānām evaiṣo 'vinayaḥ | api ca darśanamātraprasāditapuruṣāṇāṃ yuvatīnāṃ kīdṛśaṃ bhayam |

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — kiṃ ettha saṃkidavvaṃ? ṇaṃ amhāṇaṃ mahārāaṇiuttāṇaṃ jevva eso aviṇao | avi a, daṃsaṇamattappasādiapurusāṇaṃ juvaīṇaṃ kerisaṃ bhaam? (kim atra śaṅkitavyam? na cāsmākaṃ mahārājaniyuktānām evaiṣo 'vinayaḥ | api ca darśanamātraprasāditapuruṣāṇāṃ yuvatīnāṃ kīdṛśaṃ bhayam |)

    mahāmohaḥ

    vilokya | aye! saṃprāpteva priyā me mithyādṛṣṭiḥ | yāiṣā —

  • śroṇībhārabharālasā daragalanmālyopavṛtticchalāllīlotkṣiptabhujopadarśitakuconmīlannakhāṅkāvaliḥ;nīlendīvaradāmadīrghatarayā dṛṣṭyā dhayantī manodorāndolanalolakaṅkaṇajhaṇatkārottaraṃ sarpati ||

    • mahāmohaḥ — ((vilokya |)) aye! saṃprāpteva priyā me mithyādṛṣṭiḥ | yāiṣā —

    śroṇībhārabharālasā daragalanmālyopavṛtticchalāllīlotkṣiptabhujopadarśitakuconmīlannakhāṅkāvaliḥ;nīlendīvaradāmadīrghatarayā dṛṣṭyā dhayantī manodorāndolanalolakaṅkaṇajhaṇatkārottaraṃ sarpati ||
    vibhramāvatī

    eso mahārāo | uvasappadu, piasahī |eṣa mahārājaḥ | upasarpatu priyasakhī |

    vibhramāvatī — eso mahārāo | uvasappadu, piasahī | (eṣa mahārājaḥ | upasarpatu priyasakhī |)

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    upasṛtya jaadu, jaadu, mahārāo!jayatu, jayatu, mahārājaḥ!

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — ((upasṛtya))jaadu, jaadu, mahārāo! (jayatu, jayatu, mahārājaḥ!)

    mahāmohaḥ

    priye —

  • dalitakucanakhāṅkam aṅkapālīṃracaya mamāṅkam upetya pīvaroru | anuhara hariṇākṣi śaṅkarārdhasthitahimaśailasutāvilāsalakṣmīm ||

    • mithādṛṣṭiḥ sasmitaṃ tathā karoti |

    mahāmohaḥ — priye —

    dalitakucanakhāṅkam aṅkapālīṃracaya mamāṅkam upetya pīvaroru | anuhara hariṇākṣi śaṅkarārdhasthitahimaśailasutāvilāsalakṣmīm ||

    ((mithādṛṣṭiḥ sasmitaṃ tathā karoti |))

    mahāmohaḥ

    āliṅganasukham abhinīya aho, priyāyāḥ pariṣvāṅgāt parāvṛttaṃ navayauvanam | tathā hi —

  • yaḥ prāg āsīd abhinavavayovibhramāvāptajanmā,cittonmāthī vigataviṣayopaplavānandasāndraḥ,vṛttīr antas tirayati tavāśleṣajanmā sa ko 'piprauḍhapremā nava iva punar mānmatho me vikāraḥ ||

    • mahāmohaḥ — ((āliṅganasukham abhinīya)) aho, priyāyāḥ pariṣvāṅgāt parāvṛttaṃ navayauvanam | tathā hi —

    yaḥ prāg āsīd abhinavavayovibhramāvāptajanmā,cittonmāthī vigataviṣayopaplavānandasāndraḥ,vṛttīr antas tirayati tavāśleṣajanmā sa ko 'piprauḍhapremā nava iva punar mānmatho me vikāraḥ ||
    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    mahārāa, ahaṃ vi saṃpadaṃ ṇavajovvaṇā saṃvuttā | ṇa khu bhāvāṇubandho pammo kāleṇāvi vihaḍaï | āṇavedu, bhaṭṭā, kiṃṇimittaṃ bhaṭṭiṇā sumaridamhi?mahārāja, aham api sāṃprataṃ navayauvanā saṃvṛttā | na khalu bhāvānubandhaḥ premā kālenāpi vighaṭate | ājñāpayatu, bhartā, kin nimittaṃ bhartrā smṛtāsmi?

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — mahārāa, ahaṃ vi saṃpadaṃ ṇavajovvaṇā saṃvuttā | ṇa khu bhāvāṇubandho pammo kāleṇāvi vihaḍaï | āṇavedu, bhaṭṭā, kiṃṇimittaṃ bhaṭṭiṇā sumaridamhi? (mahārāja, aham api sāṃprataṃ navayauvanā saṃvṛttā | na khalu bhāvānubandhaḥ premā kālenāpi vighaṭate | ājñāpayatu, bhartā, kin nimittaṃ bhartrā smṛtāsmi?)

    mahāmohaḥ

    priye —

  • smaryate sā hi, vāmoru! cyutā yā hṛdayād bahiḥ;maccittabhittau, bhavatī, sālabhañjīva rājate ||

    • mahāmohaḥ — priye —

    smaryate sā hi, vāmoru! cyutā yā hṛdayād bahiḥ;maccittabhittau, bhavatī, sālabhañjīva rājate ||
    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    mahappasādo!mahān prasādaḥ!

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — mahappasādo! (mahān prasādaḥ!)

    mahāmohaḥ

    yathāiva prakāśitair aṅgaiḥ sarvatra vicarasi, tathāiva pravartitavyam | anyac ca — dāsyāḥ putrī śraddhā vivekena sahopaniṣadaṃ saṃyojayituṃ kuṭṭīnībhāvaṃ pratipannā | tataḥ —

  • pratikūlām akulajāṃ pāpāṃ pāpānuvartinīm —keśeṣv ākṛṣyatāṃ raṇḍāṃ pāṣaṇḍeṣu niveśaya ||

    • mahāmohaḥ — yathāiva prakāśitair aṅgaiḥ sarvatra vicarasi, tathāiva pravartitavyam | anyac ca — dāsyāḥ putrī śraddhā vivekena sahopaniṣadaṃ saṃyojayituṃ kuṭṭīnībhāvaṃ pratipannā | tataḥ —

    pratikūlām akulajāṃ pāpāṃ pāpānuvartinīm —keśeṣv ākṛṣyatāṃ raṇḍāṃ pāṣaṇḍeṣu niveśaya ||
    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    ˹eddahamettae visae alaṃ bhaṭṭiṇo ahiṇiveseṇa! vaaṇamatteṇa vva bhaṭṭiṇo dāsa vva savvo aṇṇāṃ karissadi | sā khu mae mitthā dhammo, mitthā mokkho, mitthā veamaggo, mitthā suhavigghaarāiṃ sātthapalavidāiṃ, mitthā saggaphalaṃ ti bhaṇiantī veamaggaṃ jevva parihalissadi, kiṃ uṇa uvaṇisadam | avi a —

  • visaāṇandavimukke mokkhe dosāṇa daṃsaantīe ,uvaṇisaā hi virattā jhatti karijjaï mae saddhā |˼(etāvanmātre viṣaye alaṃ bhartur abhiniveśena! vacanamātreṇaiva bhartur dāsa iva sarva ājñāṃ kariṣyati | sā khalu mayā mithyā dharmo mithyā mokṣō mithyā vedamārgo mithyā sukhavighnakarāṇi mithyā śāstrapralapitāni mithyā svargaphalam iti bhaṇyamāna vedamārgam eva parihariṣyati kiṃ punar upaniṣadam | api ca — viṣayānandavimukte mokṣe doṣān darśayantyā | upaniṣadā hi viraktā jhaṭiti krīyate mayā śraddhā |)

    • mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — ˹eddahamettae visae alaṃ bhaṭṭiṇo ahiṇiveseṇa! vaaṇamatteṇa vva bhaṭṭiṇo dāsa vva savvo aṇṇāṃ karissadi | sā khu mae mitthā dhammo, mitthā mokkho, mitthā veamaggo, mitthā suhavigghaarāiṃ sātthapalavidāiṃ, mitthā saggaphalaṃ ti bhaṇiantī veamaggaṃ jevva parihalissadi, kiṃ uṇa uvaṇisadam | avi a —

    visaāṇandavimukke mokkhe dosāṇa daṃsaantīe ,uvaṇisaā hi virattā jhatti karijjaï mae saddhā |˼(etāvanmātre viṣaye alaṃ bhartur abhiniveśena! vacanamātreṇaiva bhartur dāsa iva sarva ājñāṃ kariṣyati | sā khalu mayā mithyā dharmo mithyā mokṣō mithyā vedamārgo mithyā sukhavighnakarāṇi mithyā śāstrapralapitāni mithyā svargaphalam iti bhaṇyamāna vedamārgam eva parihariṣyati kiṃ punar upaniṣadam | api ca — viṣayānandavimukte mokṣe doṣān darśayantyā | upaniṣadā hi viraktā jhaṭiti krīyate mayā śraddhā |)
    mahārājaḥ

    yady evaṃ suṣṭhu priyaṃ me saṃpāditaṃ priyayā | punar āliṅgya cumbati |

    mahārājaḥ — yady evaṃ suṣṭhu priyaṃ me saṃpāditaṃ priyayā | ((punar āliṅgya cumbati |))
