    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ

    hanta! paāse evvaṃ paütteṇa bhattuṇā lajjemi |hanta! prakāśa evaṃ pravṛttena bhartrā lajje |

    mithyādṛṣṭiḥ — hanta! paāse evvaṃ paütteṇa bhattuṇā lajjemi | (hanta! prakāśa evaṃ pravṛttena bhartrā lajje |)

    mahāmohaḥ

    tad bhavatu! svāgāram eva praviśāmaḥ | iti niṣkrāntāḥ sarve | iti śrīkṛṣṇamiśrayativiracite prabodhacandrodaye mahāmohapradhāno nāma divtīyo 'aṅkaḥ |

    mahāmohaḥ — tad bhavatu! svāgāram eva praviśāmaḥ | ((iti niṣkrāntāḥ sarve |)) iti śrīkṛṣṇamiśrayativiracite prabodhacandrodaye mahāmohapradhāno nāma divtīyo 'aṅkaḥ |

    § 3

    p.3, l.1

    (p.3, l.1)tataḥ praviśati śāntiḥ karuṇā ca

    ((tataḥ praviśati śāntiḥ karuṇā ca))

    śāntiḥ

    sāsram mātar, mātaḥ! kvāsi? dehi me prativacanam |

  • muktātaṅkakuraṅgakā vanabhuvaḥ, śailāḥ skhaladvārayaḥ,puṇyāny āyatanāni, santatataponiṣṭhāś ca vaikhānasāḥ —yasyāḥ prītīr amīṣu, sādya bhavatī caṇḍālaveśmodaraṃnītā gauḥ kapileva jīvati kathaṃ pāṣaṇḍahastaṃ gatā?

    • athavālaṃ jīvitasaṃbhāvanayā! yataḥ,

  • mām anālokya, na snāti, na bhuṅkte, na pibaty apaḥ | na mayā rahitā śraddhā muhūrtam api jīvati ||

    • tad vinā śraddhayā muhūrtam api śānter jīvitaṃ viḍambanam eva | tat sakhi, karuṇe, madarthaṃ citām āracaya! yāvad aciram eva hutāśanapraveśena tasyāḥ sahacarī bhavāmi |

    śāntiḥ — ((sāsram)) mātar, mātaḥ! kvāsi? dehi me prativacanam |

    muktātaṅkakuraṅgakā vanabhuvaḥ, śailāḥ skhaladvārayaḥ,puṇyāny āyatanāni, santatataponiṣṭhāś ca vaikhānasāḥ —yasyāḥ prītīr amīṣu, sādya bhavatī caṇḍālaveśmodaraṃnītā gauḥ kapileva jīvati kathaṃ pāṣaṇḍahastaṃ gatā?

    athavālaṃ jīvitasaṃbhāvanayā! yataḥ,

    mām anālokya, na snāti, na bhuṅkte, na pibaty apaḥ | na mayā rahitā śraddhā muhūrtam api jīvati ||

    tad vinā śraddhayā muhūrtam api śānter jīvitaṃ viḍambanam eva | tat sakhi, karuṇe, madarthaṃ citām āracaya! yāvad aciram eva hutāśanapraveśena tasyāḥ sahacarī bhavāmi |

    karuṇā

    sāsram sahi, evvaṃ visamajjolaṇajjālāvalītikkhāiṃ akkharāiṃ jappantī savvahā viluttajīviaṃ maṃ karesi | tā pasīda muhuttaaṃ dhāredu jīviaṃ, piasahī | jāva ido tado puṇṇesu assamesu muṇiaṇasamāülesu bhāīrahītiresu suṇiuṇaṃ ṇirūvamha | sā kadāi vi mahāmohabhīdā kahaṃ vi pacchaṇṇaṃ ṇivasaï |sakhi, evaṃ viṣamajvalanajvālāvalītīkṣṇāny akṣarāṇi jalpantī sarvathā viluptajīvitāṃ māṃ karoṣi | tasmāt prasīda muhūrtaṃ dhārayatu jīvitaṃ, priyasakhī | yāvad itas tataḥ puṇyeṣv āśraṃeṣu munijanasamākuleṣu bhāgīrathītīreṣu sunipuṇaṃ nirūpayāvaḥ | sā kadācid api mahāmohabhītā katham api pracchannā nivasati |

    karuṇā — ((sāsram))sahi, evvaṃ visamajjolaṇajjālāvalītikkhāiṃ akkharāiṃ jappantī savvahā viluttajīviaṃ maṃ karesi | tā pasīda muhuttaaṃ dhāredu jīviaṃ, piasahī | jāva ido tado puṇṇesu assamesu muṇiaṇasamāülesu bhāīrahītiresu suṇiuṇaṃ ṇirūvamha | sā kadāi vi mahāmohabhīdā kahaṃ vi pacchaṇṇaṃ ṇivasaï | (sakhi, evaṃ viṣamajvalanajvālāvalītīkṣṇāny akṣarāṇi jalpantī sarvathā viluptajīvitāṃ māṃ karoṣi | tasmāt prasīda muhūrtaṃ dhārayatu jīvitaṃ, priyasakhī | yāvad itas tataḥ puṇyeṣv āśraṃeṣu munijanasamākuleṣu bhāgīrathītīreṣu sunipuṇaṃ nirūpayāvaḥ | sā kadācid api mahāmohabhītā katham api pracchannā nivasati |)

    śāntiḥ

    sakhi, kiyad anviṣyate?

  • nīvārāṅkitasaikatāni saritāṃ kūlāni vaikhānasairākrāntāni samiccaṣālacamasavyāptā gṛhā yajvanām —pratyekaṃ ca nirūpitāḥ pratipadaṃ catvāra evāśramāḥ,śraddhāyāḥ kvacid apy aho sakhi mayā vārtāpi nākarṇitā ||

    • śāntiḥ — sakhi, kiyad anviṣyate?

    nīvārāṅkitasaikatāni saritāṃ kūlāni vaikhānasairākrāntāni samiccaṣālacamasavyāptā gṛhā yajvanām —pratyekaṃ ca nirūpitāḥ pratipadaṃ catvāra evāśramāḥ,śraddhāyāḥ kvacid apy aho sakhi mayā vārtāpi nākarṇitā ||
    karuṇā

    sahi, evvaṃ bhaṇāmi | jaï saccevva saddhā tado ṇa tāe īrisīṃ duggaïṃ saṃbhāvemi | ṇa khu tārisīo puṇṇamaīo tārisaṃ asaṃbhāvaṇijjaṃ vipattiṃ aṇuhondi |sakhi, evaṃ bhaṇāmi | yadi satyeva śraddhā tato na tasyā īdṛśīṃ durgatiṃ saṃbhāvayāmi | na khalu tādṛśyaḥ puṇyamayyaḥ tādṛśīṃ asaṃbhāvanīyāṃ vipattim anubhavanti |

    karuṇā — sahi, evvaṃ bhaṇāmi | jaï saccevva saddhā tado ṇa tāe īrisīṃ duggaïṃ saṃbhāvemi | ṇa khu tārisīo puṇṇamaīo tārisaṃ asaṃbhāvaṇijjaṃ vipattiṃ aṇuhondi | (sakhi, evaṃ bhaṇāmi | yadi satyeva śraddhā tato na tasyā īdṛśīṃ durgatiṃ saṃbhāvayāmi | na khalu tādṛśyaḥ puṇyamayyaḥ tādṛśīṃ asaṃbhāvanīyāṃ vipattim anubhavanti |)

    śāntiḥ

    sakhi, kin nu pratikūle vidhātari na saṃbhāvyate? tathā hi —

  • śrīr devī janakātmajā daśamukhasyāsīd gṛhe rakṣasonītā cāiva; rasātalaṃ bhagavatī pūrvaṃ trayī dānavaiḥ;gandharvasya madālasāṃ ca tanayāṃ pātālaketuś chalāddaityendro 'pajahāra — hanta! viṣamā vāmā vidher vṛttayaḥ ||

    • tad bhavatu! pāṣaṇḍālayeṣv eva tāvad anusarāvaḥ |

    śāntiḥ — sakhi, kin nu pratikūle vidhātari na saṃbhāvyate? tathā hi —

    śrīr devī janakātmajā daśamukhasyāsīd gṛhe rakṣasonītā cāiva; rasātalaṃ bhagavatī pūrvaṃ trayī dānavaiḥ;gandharvasya madālasāṃ ca tanayāṃ pātālaketuś chalāddaityendro 'pajahāra — hanta! viṣamā vāmā vidher vṛttayaḥ ||

    tad bhavatu! pāṣaṇḍālayeṣv eva tāvad anusarāvaḥ |

    karuṇā

    sahi, evaṃ hodu |sakhy evaṃ bhavatu |

    iti parikrāmataḥ |

    karuṇā — sahi, evaṃ hodu | (sakhy evaṃ bhavatu |)

    ((iti parikrāmataḥ |))

    karuṇā

    satrāsam sahi, rakkhaso, rakkhaso!sakhi, rākṣaso, rākṣasaḥ!

    karuṇā — ((satrāsam))sahi, rakkhaso, rakkhaso! (sakhi, rākṣaso, rākṣasaḥ!)

    śāntiḥ

    kvāsau rākṣasaḥ?

    śāntiḥ — kvāsau rākṣasaḥ?

    karuṇā

    pekkha, pekkha! jo eso galantamalapaṅkapicchilabībhacchaduppekkhedahacchaī! ulluṃchiaciurabharo mukkavasaṇavesaduddaṃsaṇo! sihisihaṇḍapiṃcchiāhattho | ido jevva ahivaṭṭadi |paśya, paśya! ya eṣa galanmalapaṅkapicchilabībhatsaduḥprekṣyadehacchavir ulluñchitacikurabharo muktavasanaveṣadurdarśanaḥ śikhiśikhaṇḍapicchikāhasta ita evābhivartate |

    karuṇā — pekkha, pekkha! jo eso galantamalapaṅkapicchilabībhacchaduppekkhedahacchaī! ulluṃchiaciurabharo mukkavasaṇavesaduddaṃsaṇo! sihisihaṇḍapiṃcchiāhattho | ido jevva ahivaṭṭadi | (paśya, paśya! ya eṣa galanmalapaṅkapicchilabībhatsaduḥprekṣyadehacchavir ulluñchitacikurabharo muktavasanaveṣadurdarśanaḥ śikhiśikhaṇḍapicchikāhasta ita evābhivartate |)

    śāntiḥ

    sakhi, nāyaṃ rākṣasaḥ | nirvīryaḥ khalv ayam |

    śāntiḥ — sakhi, nāyaṃ rākṣasaḥ | nirvīryaḥ khalv ayam |

    karuṇā

    tā ko eso bhavissadi?tarhi ka eṣa bhaviṣyati |

    karuṇā — tā ko eso bhavissadi? (tarhi ka eṣa bhaviṣyati |)

    śāntiḥ

    sakhi, piśāca iti śaṅke?

    śāntiḥ — sakhi, piśāca iti śaṅke?

    karuṇā

    sahi, evvaṃ papphurantamaūhamālobbhāsiabhuaṇ'antarāe jalantappacaṇḍamaccaṇḍamaṇḍale diahamuhe kahaṃ pisāāṇaṃ avaāso?sakhi, evaṃ prasphuranmayūkhamālodbhāsitabhuvanāntarāle jvalatpracaṇḍamārtāṇḍamaṇḍale divasamukhe kathaṃ piśācānām avakāśaḥ?

    karuṇā — sahi, evvaṃ papphurantamaūhamālobbhāsiabhuaṇ'antarāe jalantappacaṇḍamaccaṇḍamaṇḍale diahamuhe kahaṃ pisāāṇaṃ avaāso? (sakhi, evaṃ prasphuranmayūkhamālodbhāsitabhuvanāntarāle jvalatpracaṇḍamārtāṇḍamaṇḍale divasamukhe kathaṃ piśācānām avakāśaḥ?)

    śāntiḥ

    tarhi anantaram eva narakavivarād uttīrṇaḥ ko 'pi nārakī bhaviṣyati! vilokya vicintya ca āḥ, jñātam! mahāmohapravartito 'yaṃ digambarasiddhāntaḥ | tat sarvathā dūre pariharaṇīyam asya darśanam | iti parāṅmukhībhavati

    śāntiḥ — tarhi anantaram eva narakavivarād uttīrṇaḥ ko 'pi nārakī bhaviṣyati! ((vilokya vicintya ca)) āḥ, jñātam! mahāmohapravartito 'yaṃ digambarasiddhāntaḥ | tat sarvathā dūre pariharaṇīyam asya darśanam | ((iti parāṅmukhībhavati ))

    karuṇā

    sahi, muhuttakaṃ ciṭṭha, jāva ido saddhāṃ aṇṇesāmi |sakhi, muhūrtaṃ tiṣṭha | yāvad itaḥ śraddhām anveṣayāmi | ubhe tathā sthite |

    tataḥ praviśati yathānirdiṣṭo digambarasiddhāntaḥ |

    karuṇā — sahi, muhuttakaṃ ciṭṭha, jāva ido saddhāṃ aṇṇesāmi | (sakhi, muhūrtaṃ tiṣṭha | yāvad itaḥ śraddhām anveṣayāmi |)((ubhe tathā sthite)) |

    ((tataḥ praviśati yathānirdiṣṭo digambarasiddhāntaḥ |))

    digambaraḥ

    ˹ṇamo aluhantāṇam, aluhantāṇam! ṇavaduvālagharamajjhe appā divavva palittae | ese jiṇavalabhāsido palamattho mokkhasukkado dhammo! iti parikrāmati | ākāśe | le le sāvaā! suṇāha, suṇāha!

  • malamaapuggalapiṇḍe saalajalehiṃ vi kelisī suddhī?appā vimalasahāvo lisipalicalaṇehi jāṇavvo ||

    • kiṃ bhaṇāha, kelisaṃ lisipalicalaṇaṃ ti? taṃ suṇāha!

  • dūle calaṇapaṇāmo, kidasakkālaṃ ca bhoaṇam miṭṭham,issāmalaṃ ṇa kajjaṃ, lisiṇaṃ dālaṃ lamantāṇam ||

    • nepathyābhimukham avalokya saddhe, ido dāva˼(namo 'rhadbhyo, 'rhadbhyaḥ! navadvāragṛhamadhye ātmā dīpa iva pradīptaḥ | eṣa jinavarabhāṣitaḥ paramārtho dharmo mokṣasaukhyadaḥ! re re śrāvakāḥ! śṛṇuta, śrṇuta!

  • malamayapudgalapiṇḍe sakalajalair api kīdṛśī śuddhiḥ?ātmā vimalasvabhāva ṛṣiparicaraṇair jñātavyaḥ ||

    • kiṃ bhaṇatha, kīdṛśam ṛṣiparicaraṇam iti? tac chṛṇuta!

  • dūre caraṇapraṇāmaḥ, kṛtasatkāraṃ ca bhojanaṃ mṛṣṭam,īrṣyāmalaṃ na kāryam, ṛṣīṇāṃ dārān ramamāṇānām ||

    • śraddhe, itas tāvat |) ubhe sabhayam ālokayataḥ | tataḥ pravśati tadanurūpaveṣā śraddhā

    digambaraḥ — ˹ṇamo aluhantāṇam, aluhantāṇam! ṇavaduvālagharamajjhe appā divavva palittae | ese jiṇavalabhāsido palamattho mokkhasukkado dhammo! (( iti parikrāmati | ākāśe |)) le le sāvaā! suṇāha, suṇāha!

    malamaapuggalapiṇḍe saalajalehiṃ vi kelisī suddhī?appā vimalasahāvo lisipalicalaṇehi jāṇavvo ||

    kiṃ bhaṇāha, kelisaṃ lisipalicalaṇaṃ ti? taṃ suṇāha!

    dūle calaṇapaṇāmo, kidasakkālaṃ ca bhoaṇam miṭṭham,issāmalaṃ ṇa kajjaṃ, lisiṇaṃ dālaṃ lamantāṇam ||

    ((nepathyābhimukham avalokya)) saddhe, ido dāva˼(namo 'rhadbhyo, 'rhadbhyaḥ! navadvāragṛhamadhye ātmā dīpa iva pradīptaḥ | eṣa jinavarabhāṣitaḥ paramārtho dharmo mokṣasaukhyadaḥ! re re śrāvakāḥ! śṛṇuta, śrṇuta!

    malamayapudgalapiṇḍe sakalajalair api kīdṛśī śuddhiḥ?ātmā vimalasvabhāva ṛṣiparicaraṇair jñātavyaḥ ||

    kiṃ bhaṇatha, kīdṛśam ṛṣiparicaraṇam iti? tac chṛṇuta!

    dūre caraṇapraṇāmaḥ, kṛtasatkāraṃ ca bhojanaṃ mṛṣṭam,īrṣyāmalaṃ na kāryam, ṛṣīṇāṃ dārān ramamāṇānām ||

    śraddhe, itas tāvat |) ((ubhe sabhayam ālokayataḥ | tataḥ pravśati tadanurūpaveṣā śraddhā))

    śraddhā

    kiṃ āṇavei lāaulaṃ?kim ājñāpayati rājakulam? śāntir mūrcchitā patati

    śraddhā — kiṃ āṇavei lāaulaṃ? (kim ājñāpayati rājakulam?)((śāntir mūrcchitā patati))

    digambarasiddhāntaḥ

    sāvaāṇaṃ kuḍumbaṃ muhuttaṃ pi mā paliccaa |śrāvakāṇāṃ kuṭumbaaṃ muhūrtam api mā parityaja |

    digambarasiddhāntaḥ — sāvaāṇaṃ kuḍumbaṃ muhuttaṃ pi mā paliccaa | (śrāvakāṇāṃ kuṭumbaaṃ muhūrtam api mā parityaja |)

    śraddhā

    jaṃ āṇavei lāaulamyad ājñāpayati rājakulam | iti niṣkrāntā

    śraddhā — jaṃ āṇavei lāaulam (yad ājñāpayati rājakulam |)((iti niṣkrāntā))

    karuṇā

    samassasaü piasahī | ṇahu ṇāmamatteṇa piasahīe bhedavvaṃ | jado sudaṃ mae ahiṃsāe saāsādo jaṃ atthi pāsaṇḍāṇaṃ vi tamassa sudā «saddhe» ti | teṇa esā tāmasī saddhā bhavissadi |samāśvasitu priyasakhī | na khalu nāmamātreṇa priyasakhyā bhetavyam | yataḥ śrutaṃ mayā ahiṃsāyāḥ sakāśād asti pāṣaṇḍānām api tamasaḥ sutā śraddheti | tenaiṣā tāmasī śraddhā bhaviṣyati |

    karuṇā — samassasaü piasahī | ṇahu ṇāmamatteṇa piasahīe bhedavvaṃ | jado sudaṃ mae ahiṃsāe saāsādo jaṃ atthi pāsaṇḍāṇaṃ vi tamassa sudā «saddhe» ti | teṇa esā tāmasī saddhā bhavissadi | (samāśvasitu priyasakhī | na khalu nāmamātreṇa priyasakhyā bhetavyam | yataḥ śrutaṃ mayā ahiṃsāyāḥ sakāśād asti pāṣaṇḍānām api tamasaḥ sutā śraddheti | tenaiṣā tāmasī śraddhā bhaviṣyati |)

    śāntiḥ

    samāśvasya | sakhi, evam evāitat | tathā hi,

  • durācārā sadācārāṃ, durdarśā priyadarśanām,ambām anusaraty eṣā durāśā na kathaṃ cana ||

    • tad bhavatu | tāvat saugatālayeṣv apy asāv anviṣyatām | śāntikaruṇe parikrāmataḥ tataḥ praviśati pustakahasto bhikṣurūpo buddhāgamaḥ

    śāntiḥ — ((samāśvasya |)) sakhi, evam evāitat | tathā hi,

    durācārā sadācārāṃ, durdarśā priyadarśanām,ambām anusaraty eṣā durāśā na kathaṃ cana ||

    tad bhavatu | tāvat saugatālayeṣv apy asāv anviṣyatām | ((śāntikaruṇe parikrāmataḥ)) ((tataḥ praviśati pustakahasto bhikṣurūpo buddhāgamaḥ))

    bhikṣuḥ

    vicintya bho bhoḥ! upāsakāḥ!

  • sākṣāt kṣaṇakṣayina eva nirātmakāś ca,yatrārpitā bahir iva pratibhānti bhāvāḥ | sāivādhunā vigalitākhilavāsanatvād,dhīsantatiḥ sphurati nirviṣayoparāgā ||

    • parikramya punaḥ saślāgham | aho! sādhur ayaṃ saugatadharmo yatra saukhyaṃ mokṣaś ca | tathā hi —

  • āvāso layanaṃ manoharam, abhiprāyānukūlā vaṇiṅnāryo, vāñchitakālam iṣṭam aśanaṃ, śayyā mṛduprastarāḥ | śraddhāpūrvam upāsikāyuvatibhiḥ kḷptāṅgadānotsavakrīḍānandabharair vrajanti vilasajjyotsnāṅkurā rātrayaḥ ||

    • bhikṣuḥ — ((vicintya)) bho bhoḥ! upāsakāḥ!

    sākṣāt kṣaṇakṣayina eva nirātmakāś ca,yatrārpitā bahir iva pratibhānti bhāvāḥ | sāivādhunā vigalitākhilavāsanatvād,dhīsantatiḥ sphurati nirviṣayoparāgā ||

    ((parikramya punaḥ saślāgham |)) aho! sādhur ayaṃ saugatadharmo yatra saukhyaṃ mokṣaś ca | tathā hi —

    āvāso layanaṃ manoharam, abhiprāyānukūlā vaṇiṅnāryo, vāñchitakālam iṣṭam aśanaṃ, śayyā mṛduprastarāḥ | śraddhāpūrvam upāsikāyuvatibhiḥ kḷptāṅgadānotsavakrīḍānandabharair vrajanti vilasajjyotsnāṅkurā rātrayaḥ ||
    karuṇā

    sahi, ko eso? taruṇataratālatalupallavo lambantakasāapisaṅgacīracīvaro sacūḍamuṇḍiamuṇḍaveso ido jevva aḍiacchadi |sakhi, ka eṣa? taruṇataratālatarupallavo lambamānakaṣāyapiśaṅgacīracīvaro sacūḍamuṇḍitamuṇḍaveṣa ita evābhigacchati

    karuṇā — sahi, ko eso? taruṇataratālatalupallavo lambantakasāapisaṅgacīracīvaro sacūḍamuṇḍiamuṇḍaveso ido jevva aḍiacchadi | (sakhi, ka eṣa? taruṇataratālatarupallavo lambamānakaṣāyapiśaṅgacīracīvaro sacūḍamuṇḍitamuṇḍaveṣa ita evābhigacchati)

    śāntiḥ

    sakhi, buddhāgama eṣaḥ |

    śāntiḥ — sakhi, buddhāgama eṣaḥ |

    bhikṣuḥ

    ākāśe bho, bho! upāsakāḥ bhikṣavaś ca! śrūyatāṃ bhagavataḥ sugatasya vākyāmṛtam! pustakaṃ vācayati | paśyāmy ahaṃ divyena cakṣuṣā lokānāṃ sugatiṃ durgatiṃ ca | kṣaṇikāḥ sarve saṃskārāḥ | nāsty ātmā sthāyī | tasmād bhikṣuṣu dārān ākramatsu nerṣitavyam | cittamalaṃ hi tad yad īrṣyānāma | nepathyābhimukham avalokya | śraddhe! itas tāvat! praviśya śraddhā |

    bhikṣuḥ — ((ākāśe)) bho, bho! upāsakāḥ bhikṣavaś ca! śrūyatāṃ bhagavataḥ sugatasya vākyāmṛtam! ((pustakaṃ vācayati |)) paśyāmy ahaṃ divyena cakṣuṣā lokānāṃ sugatiṃ durgatiṃ ca | kṣaṇikāḥ sarve saṃskārāḥ | nāsty ātmā sthāyī | tasmād bhikṣuṣu dārān ākramatsu nerṣitavyam | cittamalaṃ hi tad yad īrṣyānāma | ((nepathyābhimukham avalokya |)) śraddhe! itas tāvat! ((praviśya śraddhā |))

    śraddhā

    āṇavedu lāaulam |ājñāpayatu rājakulam |

    śraddhā — āṇavedu lāaulam | (ājñāpayatu rājakulam |)

    bhikṣuḥ

    upāsakān bhikṣūṃś ca nirbharam āliṅgya sthīyatām!

    bhikṣuḥ — upāsakān bhikṣūṃś ca nirbharam āliṅgya sthīyatām!

    śraddhā

    jaṃ āṇavedi lāaulam |yad ājñāpayati rājakulam | iti niṣkrāntā |

    śraddhā — jaṃ āṇavedi lāaulam | (yad ājñāpayati rājakulam |)((iti niṣkrāntā |))

    śāntiḥ

    sakhi, iyam api tāmasī śraddhā |

    śāntiḥ — sakhi, iyam api tāmasī śraddhā |

    karuṇā

    evvaṃ edaṃ |evaṃ etat |

    karuṇā — evvaṃ edaṃ | (evaṃ etat |)

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    bhikṣum ālokyoccaiḥ śabdam alele! bhikkhua! ido dāva | kiṃ pi pucchissam |arere! bhikṣuka! itas tāvat | kim api pṛcchāmi |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ((bhikṣum ālokyoccaiḥ śabdam))alele! bhikkhua! ido dāva | kiṃ pi pucchissam | (arere! bhikṣuka! itas tāvat | kim api pṛcchāmi |)

    bhikṣuḥ

    sakrodham āḥ! pāpa piśācākṛte! kim evaṃ pralapasi?

    bhikṣuḥ — ((sakrodham)) āḥ! pāpa piśācākṛte! kim evaṃ pralapasi?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale, muñca koham | sācchagadaṃ pucchāmi |are, muñca krodham | śāstragataṃ pṛcchāmi |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale, muñca koham | sācchagadaṃ pucchāmi | (are, muñca krodham | śāstragataṃ pṛcchāmi |)

    bhikṣuḥ

    are, kṣapaṇaka, śāstrakathām api vetsi! bhavatu | pratīmas tāvat | upasṛtya | kiṃ pṛcchasi?

    bhikṣuḥ — are, kṣapaṇaka, śāstrakathām api vetsi! bhavatu | pratīmas tāvat | ((upasṛtya |)) kiṃ pṛcchasi?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    bhaṇa, dāva kkhaṇaviṇāsiṇā tue kassa kide vadaṃ dhālīadi?bhaṇa, tāvat kṣaṇavināśinā tvayā kasya kṛte vrataṃ dhāryate?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — bhaṇa, dāva kkhaṇaviṇāsiṇā tue kassa kide vadaṃ dhālīadi? (bhaṇa, tāvat kṣaṇavināśinā tvayā kasya kṛte vrataṃ dhāryate?)

    bhikṣuḥ

    are, śrūyatām! asmatsaṃtatipatitaḥ kaścid, vijñānalakṣaṇaḥ, samucchinnavāsano, mokṣyate |

    bhikṣuḥ — are, śrūyatām! asmatsaṃtatipatitaḥ kaścid, vijñānalakṣaṇaḥ, samucchinnavāsano, mokṣyate |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale! muccalajja! kassiṃ vi maṇṇantale ko vi mukko bhavissadi? tado de saṃpadaṃ ṇaṭṭhassa kīrisaṃ uvaālaṃ kalissadi? aṇṇaṃ vi pucchāmi — keṇa de īriso dhammo saṃdiṭṭho?are! muktalajja! kasminn api manvantare ko 'pi mukto bhaviṣyati? tatas te sāṃprataṃ naṣṭasya kīdṛśam upakāraṃ kariṣyati? anyad api pṛcchāmi | kena te īdṛśo dharma sandiṣṭaḥ?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale! muccalajja! kassiṃ vi maṇṇantale ko vi mukko bhavissadi? tado de saṃpadaṃ ṇaṭṭhassa kīrisaṃ uvaālaṃ kalissadi? aṇṇaṃ vi pucchāmi — keṇa de īriso dhammo saṃdiṭṭho? (are! muktalajja! kasminn api manvantare ko 'pi mukto bhaviṣyati? tatas te sāṃprataṃ naṣṭasya kīdṛśam upakāraṃ kariṣyati? anyad api pṛcchāmi | kena te īdṛśo dharma sandiṣṭaḥ?)

    bhikṣuḥ

    nūnaṃ, sarvajñena bhagavatā buddhenokto 'yam eva dharmaḥ |

    bhikṣuḥ — nūnaṃ, sarvajñena bhagavatā buddhenokto 'yam eva dharmaḥ |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale! savvaṇṇo buddho tti kadhaṃ tue ṇādam?are! sarvajño buddha iti kathaṃ tvayā jñātam?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale! savvaṇṇo buddho tti kadhaṃ tue ṇādam? (are! sarvajño buddha iti kathaṃ tvayā jñātam?)

    bhikṣuḥ

    nanu re, tad āgamair eva prasiddho buddhaḥ sarvajña iti |

    bhikṣuḥ — nanu re, tad āgamair eva prasiddho buddhaḥ sarvajña iti |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale! ujjiabuddhae! jaï tassa bhāsideṇa savvaṇṇattaṃ paḍivajjesi, tā ahaṃ vi savvaṃ jāṇāmi | tumaṃ pi pidupidāmahehiṃ sattapulisehiṃ me dāso tti!are! ujjhitabuddhika! yadi tasya bhāṣitena sarvajñatvaṃ pratipadyase, tasmād aham api sarvaṃ jānāmi | tvam api pitṛpitāmahaiḥ saptapuruṣair me dāsa iti!

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale! ujjiabuddhae! jaï tassa bhāsideṇa savvaṇṇattaṃ paḍivajjesi, tā ahaṃ vi savvaṃ jāṇāmi | tumaṃ pi pidupidāmahehiṃ sattapulisehiṃ me dāso tti! (are! ujjhitabuddhika! yadi tasya bhāṣitena sarvajñatvaṃ pratipadyase, tasmād aham api sarvaṃ jānāmi | tvam api pitṛpitāmahaiḥ saptapuruṣair me dāsa iti!)

    bhikṣuḥ

    sakrodham āḥ pāpa! piśāca malapaṅkadhara! kiṃ tāvad ahaṃ dāsaḥ?

    bhikṣuḥ — ((sakrodham)) āḥ pāpa! piśāca malapaṅkadhara! kiṃ tāvad ahaṃ dāsaḥ?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale! vihāladāsībhuaṅga! duṭṭhapalivvajia, diṭṭhaṃdo mae daṃsido | tā piaṃ de vissaddhaṃ bhaṇāmi — buddhāṇusāsaṇaṃ palihalia alihantāṇusāsaṇaṃ jevva aṇusalidu bhavam | diambalamadaṃ ācaledu, bhavam!are! vihāradāsībhujaṅga! duṣṭaparivrājaka, dṛṣṭānto mayā darśitaḥ | tasmāt priyaṃ te visrabdhaṃ bhaṇāmi — buddhānuśāsanaṃ parihṛtyārhatānuśāsanam evānusaratu bhavān | digambaramatam eva ācarayatu, bhavān!

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale! vihāladāsībhuaṅga! duṭṭhapalivvajia, diṭṭhaṃdo mae daṃsido | tā piaṃ de vissaddhaṃ bhaṇāmi — buddhāṇusāsaṇaṃ palihalia alihantāṇusāsaṇaṃ jevva aṇusalidu bhavam | diambalamadaṃ ācaledu, bhavam! (are! vihāradāsībhujaṅga! duṣṭaparivrājaka, dṛṣṭānto mayā darśitaḥ | tasmāt priyaṃ te visrabdhaṃ bhaṇāmi — buddhānuśāsanaṃ parihṛtyārhatānuśāsanam evānusaratu bhavān | digambaramatam eva ācarayatu, bhavān!)

    bhikṣuḥ

    āḥ pāpa! svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ, parān api nāśayitum icchasi |

  • svārājyaṃ prājyam utsṛjya loke nindyām aninditaḥ,abhivāñchati ko nāma bhavān iva piśācatām?

    • api ca, ārhato api dharmavedanaṃ kaḥ śraddadhāti?

    bhikṣuḥ — āḥ pāpa! svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ, parān api nāśayitum icchasi |

    svārājyaṃ prājyam utsṛjya loke nindyām aninditaḥ,abhivāñchati ko nāma bhavān iva piśācatām?

    api ca, ārhato api dharmavedanaṃ kaḥ śraddadhāti?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    gahaṇakkhattacālacandasullopalāadukhkhalapalamalahassāṇaṃ ādesasaṃvādadaṃsaṇeṇa ṇiluvidaṃ savvaṇṇattaṇaṃ bhaavado alihantassagrahanakṣatracāracandrasūryoparāgaduṣkaraparamarahasyānam ādeśasaṃvādadarśanena nirūpitaṃ sarvajñatvaṃ bhagavato 'rhataḥ

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — gahaṇakkhattacālacandasullopalāadukhkhalapalamalahassāṇaṃ ādesasaṃvādadaṃsaṇeṇa ṇiluvidaṃ savvaṇṇattaṇaṃ bhaavado alihantassa (grahanakṣatracāracandrasūryoparāgaduṣkaraparamarahasyānam ādeśasaṃvādadarśanena nirūpitaṃ sarvajñatvaṃ bhagavato 'rhataḥ)

    bhikṣuḥ

    are! anādipravṛttena jyotiṣātīndriyajñānena pratāritena bhavatedam atikaṣṭaṃ vratam āśritam | tathā hi —

  • jñātuṃ vapuḥparimitaḥ kṣamate trilokīṃjīvaḥ kathaṃ kathaya saṃgatim antareṇa?śaknoti kumbhanihitaḥ suśikho 'pi dīpobhāvān prakāśayitum apy udare gṛhasya?

    • tasmāl lokadvayaviruddhād ārhatamatād varaṃ sugatamatam eva, sākṣāt sukhāvaham atiramaṇīyam paśyāmaḥ |

    bhikṣuḥ — are! anādipravṛttena jyotiṣātīndriyajñānena pratāritena bhavatedam atikaṣṭaṃ vratam āśritam | tathā hi —

    jñātuṃ vapuḥparimitaḥ kṣamate trilokīṃjīvaḥ kathaṃ kathaya saṃgatim antareṇa?śaknoti kumbhanihitaḥ suśikho 'pi dīpobhāvān prakāśayitum apy udare gṛhasya?

    tasmāl lokadvayaviruddhād ārhatamatād varaṃ sugatamatam eva, sākṣāt sukhāvaham atiramaṇīyam paśyāmaḥ |

    śāntiḥ

    sakhi, anyato gacchāvaḥ |

    śāntiḥ — sakhi, anyato gacchāvaḥ |

    karuṇā

    evaṃ bhodu |evaṃ bhavatu | iti parikrāmataḥ

    karuṇā — evaṃ bhodu | (evaṃ bhavatu |)((iti parikrāmataḥ))

    śāntiḥ

    puro vilokya eṣa purastāt somasiddhāntaḥ | bhavatu, atrāpi tāvad anusarāvaḥ |

    tataḥ praviśati kāpālikarūpadhārī somasiddhāntaḥ

    śāntiḥ — ((puro vilokya)) eṣa purastāt somasiddhāntaḥ | bhavatu, atrāpi tāvad anusarāvaḥ |

    ((tataḥ praviśati kāpālikarūpadhārī somasiddhāntaḥ))

    somasiddhāntaḥ

    parikramya |

  • narāsthimālākṛtacārubhūṣaṇaḥśmaśānavāsī nṛkapālabhojanaḥ,paśyāmi yogāñjanaśuddhacakṣuṣājagan mitho bhinnam abhinnam īśvarāt ||

    • somasiddhāntaḥ — ((parikramya |))

    narāsthimālākṛtacārubhūṣaṇaḥśmaśānavāsī nṛkapālabhojanaḥ,paśyāmi yogāñjanaśuddhacakṣuṣājagan mitho bhinnam abhinnam īśvarāt ||
    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale! ko eso kāvālaṃ vadaṃ dhāledi puliso | tāe ṇaṃ pucchissam | ((upasṛtya |)) alele, kāvālia! ṇalātthimuṇḍadhāi!, kīliso tuha śokkho kīliso tuha mokkho?are! ka eṣa kāpālaṃ vrataṃ dhārayati puruṣaḥ | tad enaṃ pṛcchāmi | are, kāpālika! narāsthimuṇḍadhārin! kīdṛśaṃ tava saukhyaṃ? kīdṛśas tava mokṣaḥ?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale! ko eso kāvālaṃ vadaṃ dhāledi puliso | tāe ṇaṃ pucchissam | ((upasṛtya |)) alele, kāvālia! ṇalātthimuṇḍadhāi!, kīliso tuha śokkho kīliso tuha mokkho? (are! ka eṣa kāpālaṃ vrataṃ dhārayati puruṣaḥ | tad enaṃ pṛcchāmi | are, kāpālika! narāsthimuṇḍadhārin! kīdṛśaṃ tava saukhyaṃ? kīdṛśas tava mokṣaḥ?)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    are, kṣapaṇaka! dharmaṃ tāvad asmākam avadhāraya!

  • mastiṣkāntravasābhidhāritamahāmāṃsāhutīr juhvatāṃ!vahnau brahmakapālakalpitasurāpānena naḥ pāraṇā | sadyaḥkṛttakaṭhorakaṇṭhavigalatkīlāladhārojjvalairarcyo naḥ puruṣopahārabalibhir devo mahābhairavaḥ ||

    • kāpālīkāḥ — are, kṣapaṇaka! dharmaṃ tāvad asmākam avadhāraya!

    mastiṣkāntravasābhidhāritamahāmāṃsāhutīr juhvatāṃ!vahnau brahmakapālakalpitasurāpānena naḥ pāraṇā | sadyaḥkṛttakaṭhorakaṇṭhavigalatkīlāladhārojjvalairarcyo naḥ puruṣopahārabalibhir devo mahābhairavaḥ ||
    bhikṣuḥ

    karṇau pidhāya | buddha! buddha! aho dāruṇā dharmacaryā!

    bhikṣuḥ — ((karṇau pidhāya |)) buddha! buddha! aho dāruṇā dharmacaryā!

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    alihanta! alihanta! aho gholaṃ pāvaṃ! kāvalieṇa keṇa vi vippaladdho eva eso tti takkemi!arhan! arhan! aho ghoraṃ pāpaṃ! kāpālikena kenāpi vipralabdha evaiṣa tarkayāmi!

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — alihanta! alihanta! aho gholaṃ pāvaṃ! kāvalieṇa keṇa vi vippaladdho eva eso tti takkemi! (arhan! arhan! aho ghoraṃ pāpaṃ! kāpālikena kenāpi vipralabdha evaiṣa tarkayāmi!)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    sakrodham āḥ pāpa pākhaṇḍāpaśada! muṇḍitamuṇḍa! caṇḍālaveśa! keśaluñcaka! are! vipralambhakaḥ kila caturdaśabhuvanotpattisthitipralayapravartako vedāntasiddhāntaprasiddhavibhavo bhagavān bhavānīpatiḥ? darśayāmas tarhi dharmasyāsya mahimānam?

  • hariharasurajyeṣṭhaśreṣṭhān surān aham āhare | viyati vahatāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ ruṇadhmi gatīr api | sanaganagarīm ambhaḥpūrṇāṃ vidhāya mahīm imāṃ,kalaya sakalaṃ bhūyas toyaṃ kṣaṇena pibāmi tat ||

    • kāpālīkāḥ — ((sakrodham)) āḥ pāpa pākhaṇḍāpaśada! muṇḍitamuṇḍa! caṇḍālaveśa! keśaluñcaka! are! vipralambhakaḥ kila caturdaśabhuvanotpattisthitipralayapravartako vedāntasiddhāntaprasiddhavibhavo bhagavān bhavānīpatiḥ? darśayāmas tarhi dharmasyāsya mahimānam?

    hariharasurajyeṣṭhaśreṣṭhān surān aham āhare | viyati vahatāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ ruṇadhmi gatīr api | sanaganagarīm ambhaḥpūrṇāṃ vidhāya mahīm imāṃ,kalaya sakalaṃ bhūyas toyaṃ kṣaṇena pibāmi tat ||
    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale, kāvālia! ṇaṃ ado jevva bhaṇāmi — keṇa vi endajālieṇā māāṃ daṃsia vippaladdho tti!are, kāpālika! nanv ata eva bhaṇāmi — kenāpy aindrajālikena māyāṃ darśayitvā vipralabdha iti!

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale, kāvālia! ṇaṃ ado jevva bhaṇāmi — keṇa vi endajālieṇā māāṃ daṃsia vippaladdho tti! (are, kāpālika! nanv ata eva bhaṇāmi — kenāpy aindrajālikena māyāṃ darśayitvā vipralabdha iti!)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    āḥ pāpa! punar api parameśvaram aindrajālikam ity ākṣipasi? tan na marṣanīyam asya daurātmyam! khaḍgam ākṛṣya tad aham asya…

  • etatkarālakaravālanikṛttakaṇṭhanāloccaladbahulaphenilabudbudāughaiḥ,sārdhaṃ ḍamaḍḍamaruḍāṃkṛtihūtabhūtavargeṇa bhargagṛhiṇīṃ rudhirair dhinomi ||

    • iti khaḍgam udyacchati |

    kāpālīkāḥ — āḥ pāpa! punar api parameśvaram aindrajālikam ity ākṣipasi? tan na marṣanīyam asya daurātmyam! ((khaḍgam ākṛṣya)) tad aham asya…

    etatkarālakaravālanikṛttakaṇṭhanāloccaladbahulaphenilabudbudāughaiḥ,sārdhaṃ ḍamaḍḍamaruḍāṃkṛtihūtabhūtavargeṇa bhargagṛhiṇīṃ rudhirair dhinomi ||

    ((iti khaḍgam udyacchati |))

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    sabhayam mahābhāa! ahiṃsā palamo dhammo! hiṃsā palamo adhammo!mahābhāga! ahiṃsā paramo dharmo! hiṃsā paramo 'dharmaḥ! iti bhikṣor aṅkaṃ praviśati |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ((sabhayam))mahābhāa! ahiṃsā palamo dhammo! hiṃsā palamo adhammo! (mahābhāga! ahiṃsā paramo dharmo! hiṃsā paramo 'dharmaḥ!)((iti bhikṣor aṅkaṃ praviśati |))

    bhikṣuḥ

    kāpālikaṃ vārayan bho, bho, mahābhāga! kautukaprayuktavākkalahenāyuktam etasmiṃs tapasvini prahartum |

    bhikṣuḥ — ((kāpālikaṃ vārayan)) bho, bho, mahābhāga! kautukaprayuktavākkalahenāyuktam etasmiṃs tapasvini prahartum |

    kāpālīkāḥ

    khaḍgam pratisaṃharati

    kāpālīkāḥ — ((khaḍgam pratisaṃharati))

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    samāśvasya mahābhāo jaï saṃhalidagholalosāveso saṃvutto tado ahaṃ kiṃ vi pucchiduṃ icchemi |mahābhāgo, yadi saṃhṛtaghoraroṣāveśaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ, tato 'haṃ kim api praṣṭum icchāmi |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ((samāśvasya))mahābhāo jaï saṃhalidagholalosāveso saṃvutto tado ahaṃ kiṃ vi pucchiduṃ icchemi | (mahābhāgo, yadi saṃhṛtaghoraroṣāveśaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ, tato 'haṃ kim api praṣṭum icchāmi |)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    pṛccha, pṛccha |

    kāpālīkāḥ — pṛccha, pṛccha |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    sudo tumhāṇaṃ palamo dhammo | adha keliso sokkhamokkho tti?śruto yuṣmākaṃ paramo dharmaḥ | attha kīdṛśo mokṣa iti?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — sudo tumhāṇaṃ palamo dhammo | adha keliso sokkhamokkho tti? (śruto yuṣmākaṃ paramo dharmaḥ | attha kīdṛśo mokṣa iti?)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    śṛṇu!

  • dṛṣṭaṃ kvāpi sukhaṃ vinā na viṣayair | ānandabodhojjhitā jīvasya sthitir eva muktir upalāvasthā kathaṃ prārthyate?pārvatyāḥ pratirūpayā dayitayā sānandam āliṅgitomuktaḥ krīḍati candracūḍavapur | ity ūce mṛḍānīpatiḥ ||

    • kāpālīkāḥ — śṛṇu!

    dṛṣṭaṃ kvāpi sukhaṃ vinā na viṣayair | ānandabodhojjhitā jīvasya sthitir eva muktir upalāvasthā kathaṃ prārthyate?pārvatyāḥ pratirūpayā dayitayā sānandam āliṅgitomuktaḥ krīḍati candracūḍavapur | ity ūce mṛḍānīpatiḥ ||
    bhikṣuḥ

    mahābhāga, aśraddheyam etad avītarāgasya muktir iti |

    bhikṣuḥ — mahābhāga, aśraddheyam etad avītarāgasya muktir iti |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale, kāvālia! jaï ṇa lussasi tado bhaṇāmi | salīlī salāgī mukko a tti viluddham |are, kāpālika! yadi na ruṣyasi tato bhaṇāmi | śarīrī muktaś ceti viruddham |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale, kāvālia! jaï ṇa lussasi tado bhaṇāmi | salīlī salāgī mukko a tti viluddham | (are, kāpālika! yadi na ruṣyasi tato bhaṇāmi | śarīrī muktaś ceti viruddham |)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    svagatam aye! aśraddhākṣiptam anayor antaḥkaraṇam | bhavatv | evaṃ tāvat | prakāśam śraddhe! itas tāvat!

    tataḥ praviśati kāpālinīrūpadhāriṇī śraddhā

    kāpālīkāḥ — ((svagatam)) aye! aśraddhākṣiptam anayor antaḥkaraṇam | bhavatv | evaṃ tāvat | ((prakāśam)) śraddhe! itas tāvat!

    ((tataḥ praviśati kāpālinīrūpadhāriṇī śraddhā))

    karuṇā

    ˹sahi, pekkha! rajasas sudā saddhā | sā esā —

  • viphullaṇīl'uppalalolaloaṇā,ṇar'atthimālākidacālubhūsaṇā,ṇiambapīṇatthaṇabhālamanthalā,vihādi puṇṇendumuhī vilāsiṇī |˼(sakhi, paśya! rajasaḥ sutā śraddhā | saiṣā — viphullanīlotpalalolalocanā,narāsthimālākṛtacārubhūṣaṇā,nitambapīnastanabhāramantharā,vibhāti pūrṇendumukhī vilāsinī |)

    • karuṇā — ˹sahi, pekkha! rajasas sudā saddhā | sā esā —

    viphullaṇīl'uppalalolaloaṇā,ṇar'atthimālākidacālubhūsaṇā,ṇiambapīṇatthaṇabhālamanthalā,vihādi puṇṇendumuhī vilāsiṇī |˼(sakhi, paśya! rajasaḥ sutā śraddhā | saiṣā — viphullanīlotpalalolalocanā,narāsthimālākṛtacārubhūṣaṇā,nitambapīnastanabhāramantharā,vibhāti pūrṇendumukhī vilāsinī |)
    śraddhā

    parikramya | esa mhi! āṇavedu sāmī |eṣāsmi! ājñāpayatu svāmī |

    śraddhā — ((parikramya |))esa mhi! āṇavedu sāmī | (eṣāsmi! ājñāpayatu svāmī |)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    priye, enaṃ durabhimāninaṃ bhikṣuṃ tāvad gṛhāṇa! śraddhā bhikṣum āliṅgati

    kāpālīkāḥ — priye, enaṃ durabhimāninaṃ bhikṣuṃ tāvad gṛhāṇa! ((śraddhā bhikṣum āliṅgati))

    bhikṣuḥ

    sānandaṃ pariṣvajya, romāñcam abhinīya, janāntikam | aho! sukhasparśā kāpālinī | tathā hi —

  • raṇḍāḥ pīnapayodharāḥ kati mayā caṇḍānurāgād bhujadvandvāpīḍitapīvarastanabharaṃ no gāḍham āliṅgitāḥ?buddhebhyaḥ śataśaḥ śape mayi punaḥ kutrāpi kāpālinīpīnottuṅgakucāvagūhanabhavaḥ prāptaḥ pramododayaḥ!

    • aho! puṇyaṃ kāpālikacaritam! aho! ślāghyaḥ somasiddhāntaḥ! āścaryo 'yaṃ dharmaḥ! bho, mahābhāga! sarvathā buddhānuśāsanam asmābhir utsṛṣṭam praviṣṭāḥ smaḥ pārameśvaraṃ siddhāntam! tad ācāryas tvaṃ śiṣyo 'ham | praveśaya māṃ pārameśvarīṃ dīkṣām!

    bhikṣuḥ — ((sānandaṃ pariṣvajya, romāñcam abhinīya, janāntikam |)) aho! sukhasparśā kāpālinī | tathā hi —

    raṇḍāḥ pīnapayodharāḥ kati mayā caṇḍānurāgād bhujadvandvāpīḍitapīvarastanabharaṃ no gāḍham āliṅgitāḥ?buddhebhyaḥ śataśaḥ śape mayi punaḥ kutrāpi kāpālinīpīnottuṅgakucāvagūhanabhavaḥ prāptaḥ pramododayaḥ!

    aho! puṇyaṃ kāpālikacaritam! aho! ślāghyaḥ somasiddhāntaḥ! āścaryo 'yaṃ dharmaḥ! bho, mahābhāga! sarvathā buddhānuśāsanam asmābhir utsṛṣṭam praviṣṭāḥ smaḥ pārameśvaraṃ siddhāntam! tad ācāryas tvaṃ śiṣyo 'ham | praveśaya māṃ pārameśvarīṃ dīkṣām!

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale, bhikkhua! kāvāliṇīphalasaṇeṇa dūsido tumam | tā dūlaṃ apasala!are, bhikṣo! kāpālinīsparśanena dūṣitas tvam | tasmād dūram apasara!

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale, bhikkhua! kāvāliṇīphalasaṇeṇa dūsido tumam | tā dūlaṃ apasala! (are, bhikṣo! kāpālinīsparśanena dūṣitas tvam | tasmād dūram apasara!)

    bhikṣuḥ

    āḥ pāpa! vañcito 'si re kāpālinyāḥ parirambhamahotsavena!

    bhikṣuḥ — āḥ pāpa! vañcito 'si re kāpālinyāḥ parirambhamahotsavena!

    kāpālīkāḥ

    priye, kṣapaṇakaṃ gṛhāṇa | kāpāliṇī kṣapaṇakam āliṅgati

    kāpālīkāḥ — priye, kṣapaṇakaṃ gṛhāṇa | ((kāpāliṇī kṣapaṇakam āliṅgati))

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    saromāñcam ˹aho arihanta! aho arihanta! kāvālinīe phalasasuhaṃ! aï, sundali! dedu! dedu! dāva puṇo aṅkapāliṃ! svagatam are, mahanto khu indiaviālo saṃvutto! tā kiṃ ettha juttaṃ? bhodu | picchiāe ḍhakissam | tathā kṛtvā

  • ayi! pīṇaghaṇatthaṇasohiṇi! palitatthakulaṅgaviloalloaṇe!jaï lamasi kāvāliṇi, tā kiṃ kalissadi sāvakī?

    • aho, kāvāliaṃ jevva ekkaṃ daṃsaṇaṃ sokkhamokkhasāhaṇaṃ | bho, ācālia! ahaṃ tuha dāso saṃvutto | maṃ pi mahābhailavāṇusāsaṇe dīkkhedu!˼(aho arhanta! aho arhanta! kāpālinyāḥ sparśasukham | aye, sundari! dadātu! dadātu! tāvat punar aṅkapālim! are, mahān khalv indriyavikāra saṃvṛtttaḥ! tasmād kim atra yuktam? bhavatu | picchikayā sthagayiṣye |

  • ayi pīnaghanastanaśobhini! paritrastakuraṅgavilolalocane!yadi ramase kāpālini, tat kiṃ kariṣyati śrāvakī?

    • aho, kāpālikaṃ darśanam evaikaṃ saukhyamokṣasādhanam | bho, ācārya! ahaṃ tava dāsaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | mām api mahābhairavānuśāsane dīkṣayata!)

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ((saromāñcam)) ˹aho arihanta! aho arihanta! kāvālinīe phalasasuhaṃ! aï, sundali! dedu! dedu! dāva puṇo aṅkapāliṃ! ((svagatam)) are, mahanto khu indiaviālo saṃvutto! tā kiṃ ettha juttaṃ? bhodu | picchiāe ḍhakissam | ((tathā kṛtvā))

    ayi! pīṇaghaṇatthaṇasohiṇi! palitatthakulaṅgaviloalloaṇe!jaï lamasi kāvāliṇi, tā kiṃ kalissadi sāvakī?

    aho, kāvāliaṃ jevva ekkaṃ daṃsaṇaṃ sokkhamokkhasāhaṇaṃ | bho, ācālia! ahaṃ tuha dāso saṃvutto | maṃ pi mahābhailavāṇusāsaṇe dīkkhedu!˼(aho arhanta! aho arhanta! kāpālinyāḥ sparśasukham | aye, sundari! dadātu! dadātu! tāvat punar aṅkapālim! are, mahān khalv indriyavikāra saṃvṛtttaḥ! tasmād kim atra yuktam? bhavatu | picchikayā sthagayiṣye |

    bhaavaṃ, palipūliaṃ sulāe bhāaṇam |bhagavan, paripūritaṃ surayā bhājanam |

    śraddhā — bhaavaṃ, palipūliaṃ sulāe bhāaṇam | (bhagavan, paripūritaṃ surayā bhājanam |)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    pītvā śeṣaṃ bhikṣukṣapaṇakayor arpayati |

  • idaṃ pavitram amṛtam pīyatāṃ, bhavabheṣajam,paśupāśasamucchedakāraṇaṃ, bhairavoditam ||

    • ubhau vimṛśataḥ |

    kāpālīkāḥ — ((pītvā śeṣaṃ bhikṣukṣapaṇakayor arpayati |))

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    amhāṇaṃ alihantāṇusāsaṇe sulāpāṇaṃ ṇ'atthi |asmākam ārhatānuśāsane surāpānaṃ nāsti |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — amhāṇaṃ alihantāṇusāsaṇe sulāpāṇaṃ ṇ'atthi | (asmākam ārhatānuśāsane surāpānaṃ nāsti |)

    bhikṣuḥ

    kathaṃ kāpālikocchiṣṭāṃ surāṃ pāsyāmi?

    bhikṣuḥ — kathaṃ kāpālikocchiṣṭāṃ surāṃ pāsyāmi?

    kāpālīkāḥ

    kiñcid vimṛṣya | kiṃ vimṛśasi, śraddhe? paśutvam anayor nādyāpy apanīyate | tenāsmadvadanasaṃsargaduṣṭāṃ pavitrāṃ surām etau manyete | tad, bhavatī, svavaktrāsavapūtāṃ kṛtvānayor upanayatu | yatas tairthikā api vadanti strīmukhaṃ tu sadā śuci iti |

    kāpālīkāḥ — ((kiñcid vimṛṣya |)) kiṃ vimṛśasi, śraddhe? paśutvam anayor nādyāpy apanīyate | tenāsmadvadanasaṃsargaduṣṭāṃ pavitrāṃ surām etau manyete | tad, bhavatī, svavaktrāsavapūtāṃ kṛtvānayor upanayatu | yatas tairthikā api vadanti strīmukhaṃ tu sadā śuci iti |

    jaṃ bhaavaṃ āṇavedi!yad bhagavān ājñāpayati! iti pānapātraṃ gṛhītvā, pītaśeṣam upanayati |

    śraddhā — jaṃ bhaavaṃ āṇavedi! (yad bhagavān ājñāpayati!)((iti pānapātraṃ gṛhītvā, pītaśeṣam upanayati |))

    bhikṣuḥ

    mahān prasādaḥ! iti caṣakaṃ gṛhītvā pibati | aho! surāyāḥ saundaryam!

  • nipītā veśyābhiḥ saha na kativārān suvadanāmukhocchiṣṭāsmābhiḥ sarasamadirāmodamadhurā?kapālinyā vaktrāsavasurabhim etāṃ tu madirāmalabdhvā jānīmaḥ spṛhayati sudhāyai suragaṇaḥ ||

    • bhikṣuḥ — mahān prasādaḥ! ((iti caṣakaṃ gṛhītvā pibati |)) aho! surāyāḥ saundaryam!

    nipītā veśyābhiḥ saha na kativārān suvadanāmukhocchiṣṭāsmābhiḥ sarasamadirāmodamadhurā?kapālinyā vaktrāsavasurabhim etāṃ tu madirāmalabdhvā jānīmaḥ spṛhayati sudhāyai suragaṇaḥ ||
    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale, bhikkhua! mā savvaṃ piba! kāvāliṇīvaaṇocchiṭṭhaṃ maïlaṃ maha vi dhālaedu!are bhikṣo! mā sarvaṃ piba! kāpālinīvadanocchiṣṭāṃ madirāṃ mamāpi dhārayatu! bhikṣuḥ kṣapaṇakāya caṣakam upanayati |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale, bhikkhua! mā savvaṃ piba! kāvāliṇīvaaṇocchiṭṭhaṃ maïlaṃ maha vi dhālaedu! (are bhikṣo! mā sarvaṃ piba! kāpālinīvadanocchiṣṭāṃ madirāṃ mamāpi dhārayatu!)((bhikṣuḥ kṣapaṇakāya caṣakam upanayati |))

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    pītvā | aho, sulāe mahulattaṇam! aho, sādo! aho, gandho! aho, sulahittaṇam! cilaṃ khu alihantāṇusāsaṇe piḍido vañcido mhi ediseṇa sulālaseṇa! ale bhikkua, gholanti me aṅgāiṃ | tā uvaviśamhaaho, surāyā madhuratvam! aho, svādaḥ! aho, gandhaḥ! aho, surabhitvam! ciraṃ khalv ārhatānuśāsane patito vañcito 'smi īdṛśena surārasena! are bhikṣuka, ghūrṇanti me 'ṅgāni | tasmād upaviśāvaḥ |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ((pītvā |))aho, sulāe mahulattaṇam! aho, sādo! aho, gandho! aho, sulahittaṇam! cilaṃ khu alihantāṇusāsaṇe piḍido vañcido mhi ediseṇa sulālaseṇa! ale bhikkua, gholanti me aṅgāiṃ | tā uvaviśamha (aho, surāyā madhuratvam! aho, svādaḥ! aho, gandhaḥ! aho, surabhitvam! ciraṃ khalv ārhatānuśāsane patito vañcito 'smi īdṛśena surārasena! are bhikṣuka, ghūrṇanti me 'ṅgāni | tasmād upaviśāvaḥ |)

    bhikṣuḥ

    evaṃ kurvaḥ | tathā kurutaḥ |

    bhikṣuḥ — evaṃ kurvaḥ | ((tathā kurutaḥ |))

    kāpālīkāḥ

    priye, amūlyakrītaṃ dāsadvayaṃ labdham | tan nṛtyāvas tāvat! ubhau nṛtyataḥ |

    kāpālīkāḥ — priye, amūlyakrītaṃ dāsadvayaṃ labdham | tan nṛtyāvas tāvat! ((ubhau nṛtyataḥ |))

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale bhikkua | eso kāvālio — ahavo ācālio — kāvālinīe saddhaṃ sohaṇaṃ ṇaccedi | tā edāe saddhaṃ amhe vi ṇaccāmha!are bhikṣuka | eṣa kāpāliko — 'thavācāryaḥ — kāpālinyā sārdhaṃ śobhanaṃ nṛtyati | tasmād etābhyāṃ sahāvām api nṛtyāvaḥ!

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale bhikkua | eso kāvālio — ahavo ācālio — kāvālinīe saddhaṃ sohaṇaṃ ṇaccedi | tā edāe saddhaṃ amhe vi ṇaccāmha! (are bhikṣuka | eṣa kāpāliko — 'thavācāryaḥ — kāpālinyā sārdhaṃ śobhanaṃ nṛtyati | tasmād etābhyāṃ sahāvām api nṛtyāvaḥ!)

    bhikṣuḥ

    ācārya, mahāścaryam etad darśanaṃ! yatrākleśam abhimatārthasiddhayaḥ saṃpadyante! madaskhalitaṃ nṛtyataḥ |

    bhikṣuḥ — ācārya, mahāścaryam etad darśanaṃ! yatrākleśam abhimatārthasiddhayaḥ saṃpadyante! ((madaskhalitaṃ nṛtyataḥ |))

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ˹«ayi pīṇaghaṇi…»˼ ity ādi gāyati

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ((˹«ayi pīṇaghaṇi…»˼ ity ādi gāyati))

    kāpālīkāḥ

    kiyad etad āścaryaṃ paśya!

  • yatrānujjhitavāñchitārthaviṣayāsaṅge 'pi sidhyanty amūḥpratyāsannamahodayapraṇayinām aṣṭau mahāsiddhayaḥ,vaśyākarṣavimohanapramathanaprakṣobhaṇoccāṭanaprāyaḥ prākṛtasiddhayas tu viduṣāṃ yogāntarāyāḥ param ||

    • kāpālīkāḥ — kiyad etad āścaryaṃ paśya!

    yatrānujjhitavāñchitārthaviṣayāsaṅge 'pi sidhyanty amūḥpratyāsannamahodayapraṇayinām aṣṭau mahāsiddhayaḥ,vaśyākarṣavimohanapramathanaprakṣobhaṇoccāṭanaprāyaḥ prākṛtasiddhayas tu viduṣāṃ yogāntarāyāḥ param ||
    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    ale kāpālia, ((vimṛśya)) ahava ācālia, ācālialāa, kulācālia |are kāpālika, athavā ācārya, ācāryarāja, kulācārya |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ale kāpālia, ((vimṛśya)) ahava ācālia, ācālialāa, kulācālia | (are kāpālika, athavā ācārya, ācāryarāja, kulācārya |)

    bhikṣuḥ

    vihasya ayam anabhyāsātiśayapītayā madirayā dūram unmattīkṛtas tapasvī! tat kriyatām asya madāpanayanam!

    bhikṣuḥ — ((vihasya)) ayam anabhyāsātiśayapītayā madirayā dūram unmattīkṛtas tapasvī! tat kriyatām asya madāpanayanam!

    kāpālīkāḥ

    evaṃ bhavatu | iti svamukhocchiṣṭaṃ tāmbūlaṃ kṣapaṇakāya dadāti

    kāpālīkāḥ — evaṃ bhavatu | ((iti svamukhocchiṣṭaṃ tāmbūlaṃ kṣapaṇakāya dadāti))

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    saṃjñāṃ labdhvā kṣaṇaṃ svasthībhūya | ācāliaṃ evva edaṃ pucchissam | jādisī tuha sulāe āhalaṇattī kiṃ tādisī itthiāpulisesu vi atthi?ācāryam ev' aitat pṛcchāmi | yādṛśī tava surāyā āharaṇaśaktiḥ kiṃ tādṛśī strīpuruṣeṣv apy asti?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — ((saṃjñāṃ labdhvā kṣaṇaṃ svasthībhūya |))ācāliaṃ evva edaṃ pucchissam | jādisī tuha sulāe āhalaṇattī kiṃ tādisī itthiāpulisesu vi atthi? (ācāryam ev' aitat pṛcchāmi | yādṛśī tava surāyā āharaṇaśaktiḥ kiṃ tādṛśī strīpuruṣeṣv apy asti?)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    kiṃ viśeṣeṇa pṛcchyate? paśya —

  • vidyādhārīṃ vātha surāṅganāṃ vā,nāgāṅganāṃ vāpy atha yakṣakanyām,yad yan mameṣṭaṃ bhuvanatraye 'pividyābalāt tat tad upāharāmi ||

    • kāpālīkāḥ — kiṃ viśeṣeṇa pṛcchyate? paśya —

    vidyādhārīṃ vātha surāṅganāṃ vā,nāgāṅganāṃ vāpy atha yakṣakanyām,yad yan mameṣṭaṃ bhuvanatraye 'pividyābalāt tat tad upāharāmi ||
    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    bho, edaṃ mae gaṇideṇa ṇṇādaṃ — jaṃ savve amhe mahālāamahāmohassa kiṃkale tti |bho, etan mayā gaṇitena jñātam — yat sarve vayaṃ mahārājamahāmohasya kiṃkarā iti |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — bho, edaṃ mae gaṇideṇa ṇṇādaṃ — jaṃ savve amhe mahālāamahāmohassa kiṃkale tti | (bho, etan mayā gaṇitena jñātam — yat sarve vayaṃ mahārājamahāmohasya kiṃkarā iti |)

    ubhau

    yathājñātam āyuṣmatā, evam etat |

    ubhau — yathājñātam āyuṣmatā, evam etat |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    tā lāakajjaṃ mantīyadu |tasmād rājakāryaṃ mantrayatām

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — tā lāakajjaṃ mantīyadu | (tasmād rājakāryaṃ mantrayatām)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    kiṃ tat?

    kāpālīkāḥ — kiṃ tat?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    sattassa sudā saddhā mahālāassa aṇṇāe āhalaṇīe tti |sattvasya sutā śraddhā mahārājasyājñayāharaṇiyeti |

    kṣapaṇakaḥ — sattassa sudā saddhā mahālāassa aṇṇāe āhalaṇīe tti | (sattvasya sutā śraddhā mahārājasyājñayāharaṇiyeti |)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    kathaya kvāsau dāsyāḥ putrī? eṣa tām aciram eva vidyābalād upāharāmi | kṣapaṇakaḥ khaṇḍinīm ādāya gaṇayati

    kāpālīkāḥ — kathaya kvāsau dāsyāḥ putrī? eṣa tām aciram eva vidyābalād upāharāmi | ((kṣapaṇakaḥ khaṇḍinīm ādāya gaṇayati))

    śāntiḥ

    sakhi, ambām uddviśyāiva hatāśānām ālāpaḥ śṛṇomi; tad avadhānena tāvad ākarṇayāvaḥ |

    gāthāṃ gaṇayitvā |

  • ˹ṇatthi jale, ṇatthi vaṇe, ṇatthi gilibilesu, ṇatthi pāāle,sā viṇṇubhattisahidā ṇivasadi hiae mahappāṇam |˼( nāsti jale, nāsti vane, nāsti giribileṣu, nāsti pātāle,sā viṣṇubhaktisahitā nivasati hṛdaye mahātmanām |)

    karuṇā

    sānandam sahi, diṭṭhiā vaḍḍhasi | sudaṃ viṇṇubhattīe devīe pāsavaṭṭiṇī saddhe tti |sakhi, diṣṭyā vardhase | śrutaṃ viṣṇubhaktyā devyāḥ pārśvavartinī śraddheti | śāntiḥ harṣaṃ nāṭayati |

    bhikṣuḥ

    atha dharmasya kāmād apakrāntasya kutra pravṛttiḥ?

    bhikṣuḥ — atha dharmasya kāmād apakrāntasya kutra pravṛttiḥ?

    kṣapaṇakaḥ

    punar gaṇayitvā

  • ˹ṇatthi jale, ṇatthi vaṇe, ṇatthi gilibilesu, ṇatthi pāāle,sā viṇṇubhattisahido vatta hiae mahappāṇam |˼( nāsti jale, nāsti vane, nāsti giribileṣu, nāsti pātāle,sa viṣṇubhaktisahito vartate hṛdaye mahātmanām |)

    kāpālīkāḥ

    saviṣādam aho mahat kaṣṭam āpatitaṃ mahārājasya! tathā hi —

  • mūlaṃ devī siddhaye viṣṇubhaktis,tāṃ ca śraddhānuvratā sattvakanyā;kāmān muktas tatra dharmo 'py abhūc cet,siddhaṃ manye tad vivekasya sādhyam ||

    • tathāpi tāvad asuvyayenāpi svāminaḥ prayojanam anuṣṭheyam | tan mahābhairavīṃ vidyāṃ dharmaśraddhayor āharaṇāya prasthāpayāmaḥ | iti niṣkrāntāḥ

    kāpālīkāḥ — ((saviṣādam)) aho mahat kaṣṭam āpatitaṃ mahārājasya! tathā hi —

    mūlaṃ devī siddhaye viṣṇubhaktis,tāṃ ca śraddhānuvratā sattvakanyā;kāmān muktas tatra dharmo 'py abhūc cet,siddhaṃ manye tad vivekasya sādhyam ||

    tathāpi tāvad asuvyayenāpi svāminaḥ prayojanam anuṣṭheyam | tan mahābhairavīṃ vidyāṃ dharmaśraddhayor āharaṇāya prasthāpayāmaḥ | ((iti niṣkrāntāḥ))

    śāntiḥ

    āvām apy evaṃ hatāśānāṃ vyavasāyaṃ devyai viṣṇubhaktyai nivedayāvaḥ | iti niṣkrāntāḥ sarve iti śrīkṛṣṇamiśrayativiracite prabodhacandrodaye pāṣaṇḍaviḍambhano nāma tṛtīyo 'ṅkaḥ |

    śāntiḥ — āvām apy evaṃ hatāśānāṃ vyavasāyaṃ devyai viṣṇubhaktyai nivedayāvaḥ | ((iti niṣkrāntāḥ sarve)) iti śrīkṛṣṇamiśrayativiracite prabodhacandrodaye pāṣaṇḍaviḍambhano nāma tṛtīyo 'ṅkaḥ |

    § 4

    p.4, l.1

    (p.4, l.1)tataḥ praviśati maitrī |

    ((tataḥ praviśati maitrī |))

    maitrī

    sudaṃ mae mudiāsaāsādo jaṃ mahābhairavīkahaḍhaṇasambhamādo bhaavadīe viṇṇubhattīe parittādā piasahī saddheti | tā ukkaṇṭhieṇa hiaeṇa piasahīṃ pekkhissam |śrutaṃ mayā muditāsakāśād yan mahābhairavīkarṣaṇasaṃbhramato bhagavatyā viṣṇubhaktyā paritrātā priyasakhī śraddheti | tasmād utkaṇṭhitena hṛdayena priyasakhīṃ prekṣiṣye | parikrāmati tataḥ praviśati śraddhā |

    maitrī — sudaṃ mae mudiāsaāsādo jaṃ mahābhairavīkahaḍhaṇasambhamādo bhaavadīe viṇṇubhattīe parittādā piasahī saddheti | tā ukkaṇṭhieṇa hiaeṇa piasahīṃ pekkhissam | (śrutaṃ mayā muditāsakāśād yan mahābhairavīkarṣaṇasaṃbhramato bhagavatyā viṣṇubhaktyā paritrātā priyasakhī śraddheti | tasmād utkaṇṭhitena hṛdayena priyasakhīṃ prekṣiṣye |)((parikrāmati))((tataḥ praviśati śraddhā |))

    śraddhā

    sabhayotkampam

  • ghorāṃ, nārakapālakuṇḍalavatīṃ, vidyucchaṭā dṛṣṭibhirmuñcantīṃ, vikarālamūrtim analajvālapiśaṅgaiḥ kacaiḥ | daṃṣṭrācandrakalāṅkurāntaravalajjihvāṃ mahābhairavīṃpaśyantyā iva, me manaḥ kadalikevādyāpy aho vepate ||

    • śraddhā — ((sabhayotkampam))

    ghorāṃ, nārakapālakuṇḍalavatīṃ, vidyucchaṭā dṛṣṭibhirmuñcantīṃ, vikarālamūrtim analajvālapiśaṅgaiḥ kacaiḥ | daṃṣṭrācandrakalāṅkurāntaravalajjihvāṃ mahābhairavīṃpaśyantyā iva, me manaḥ kadalikevādyāpy aho vepate ||
    maitrī

    svagatam ae! esā me piasahī bhaasambhāntahiaā, kalidakampataralehiṃ aṅgehiṃ kiṃ vi mantaantī | saṃmuhāadaṃ vi maṃ ṇa lakkhedi! ālavissaṃ dāva | ((prakāśam)) piasahi, saddhe! kisa tumaṃ uttāviahiaā maṃ vi ṇa āloesi?aye! eṣā me priyasakhī bhayasambhrāntahṛdayākalitakampataralair aṅgaiḥ kiṃ api mantrayantī saṃmukhāgatām api māṃ na lakṣayatī! ālapiṣye tāvat | priyasakhi, śraddhe! kasmāt tvam uttāpitahṛdayā mām api nālokayasi?

    maitrī — ((svagatam))ae! esā me piasahī bhaasambhāntahiaā, kalidakampataralehiṃ aṅgehiṃ kiṃ vi mantaantī | saṃmuhāadaṃ vi maṃ ṇa lakkhedi! ālavissaṃ dāva | ((prakāśam)) piasahi, saddhe! kisa tumaṃ uttāviahiaā maṃ vi ṇa āloesi? (aye! eṣā me priyasakhī bhayasambhrāntahṛdayākalitakampataralair aṅgaiḥ kiṃ api mantrayantī saṃmukhāgatām api māṃ na lakṣayatī! ālapiṣye tāvat | priyasakhi, śraddhe! kasmāt tvam uttāpitahṛdayā mām api nālokayasi?)

    śraddhā

    vilokya socchvāsam aye! me priyasakhī maitrī!

  • kālarātrikarālāsyadantāntargatayā mayā,dṛṣṭāsi sakhi sāiva tvaṃ punar atrāiva janmani ||

    • tad ehi pariṣvajasva mām!

    śraddhā — ((vilokya socchvāsam)) aye! me priyasakhī maitrī!

    kālarātrikarālāsyadantāntargatayā mayā,dṛṣṭāsi sakhi sāiva tvaṃ punar atrāiva janmani ||

    maitrī — ((tathā kṛtvā))sahi, taha viṇṇubhattiṇibbhatthidappabhāvāe mahābhairavīe kaḍḍhaṇasambhamādo ajja vi vevandi de aṅgāi | (sakhi, tathā viṣṇubhaktinirbhartsitaprabhāvayā mahābhairavyāḥ karṣaṇasambhramato 'dyāpi vepante te 'ṅgāni |)
